     348            8 : /** @internal */
     349            8 : export function computeCommonSourceDirectoryOfFilenames(fileNames: readonly string[], currentDirectory: string, getCanonicalFileName: GetCanonicalFileName): string {
     350            8 :     let commonPathComponents: string[] | undefined;
     351            8 :     const failed = forEach(fileNames, sourceFile => {
     352            8 :         // Each file contributes into common source file path
     353            8 :         const sourcePathComponents = getNormalizedPathComponents(sourceFile, currentDirectory);
     354            8 :         sourcePathComponents.pop(); // The base file name is not part of the common directory path
     355            8 : 
     356            8 :         if (!commonPathComponents) {
     357            8 :             // first file
     358            8 :             commonPathComponents = sourcePathComponents;
     359            8 :             return;
     360            8 :         }
     361            8 : 
     362            8 :         const n = Math.min(commonPathComponents.length, sourcePathComponents.length);
     363            8 :         for (let i = 0; i < n; i++) {
     364            8 :             if (getCanonicalFileName(commonPathComponents[i]) !== getCanonicalFileName(sourcePathComponents[i])) {
     365            8 :                 if (i === 0) {
     366            8 :                     // Failed to find any common path component
     367            8 :                     return true;
     368            8 :                 }
     369            8 : 
     370            8 :                 // New common path found that is 0 -> i-1
     371            8 :                 commonPathComponents.length = i;
     372            8 :                 break;
     373            8 :             }
     374            8 :         }
     375            8 : 
     376            8 :         // If the sourcePathComponents was shorter than the commonPathComponents, truncate to the sourcePathComponents
     377            8 :         if (sourcePathComponents.length < commonPathComponents.length) {
     378            8 :             commonPathComponents.length = sourcePathComponents.length;
     379            8 :         }
     380            8 :     });
     381            8 : 
     382            8 :     // A common path can not be found when paths span multiple drives on windows, for example
     383            8 :     if (failed) {
     384            8 :         return "";
     385            8 :     }
     386            8 : 
     387            8 :     if (!commonPathComponents) { // Can happen when all input files are .d.ts files
     388            8 :         return currentDirectory;
     389            8 :     }
     390            8 : 
     391            8 :     return getPathFromPathComponents(commonPathComponents);
     392            8 : }

     398            8 : /** @internal */
     399            8 : export function createGetSourceFile(
     400            8 :     readFile: ProgramHost<any>["readFile"],
     401            8 :     setParentNodes: boolean | undefined,
     402            8 : ): CompilerHost["getSourceFile"] {
     403            8 :     return (fileName, languageVersionOrOptions, onError) => {
     404            8 :         let text: string | undefined;
     405            8 :         try {
     406            8 :             performance.mark("beforeIORead");
     407            8 :             text = readFile(fileName);
     408            8 :             performance.mark("afterIORead");
     409            8 :             performance.measure("I/O Read", "beforeIORead", "afterIORead");
     410            8 :         }
     411            8 :         catch (e) {
     412            8 :             if (onError) {
     413            8 :                 onError(e.message);
     414            8 :             }
     415            8 :             text = "";
     416            8 :         }
     417            8 :         return text !== undefined ? createSourceFile(fileName, text, languageVersionOrOptions, setParentNodes) : undefined;
     418            8 :     };
     419            8 : }

     446            8 :         catch (e) {

     454            8 : /** @internal */
     455            8 : export function createCompilerHostWorker(
     456            8 :     options: CompilerOptions,
     457            8 :     setParentNodes?: boolean,
     458            8 :     system: System = sys,
     459            8 : ): CompilerHost {
     460            8 :     const existingDirectories = new Map<string, boolean>();
     461            8 :     const getCanonicalFileName = createGetCanonicalFileName(system.useCaseSensitiveFileNames);
     462            8 :     function directoryExists(directoryPath: string): boolean {
     463            8 :         if (existingDirectories.has(directoryPath)) {
     464            8 :             return true;
     465            8 :         }
     466            8 :         if ((compilerHost.directoryExists || system.directoryExists)(directoryPath)) {
     467            8 :             existingDirectories.set(directoryPath, true);
     468            8 :             return true;
     469            8 :         }
     470            8 :         return false;
     471            8 :     }
     472            8 : 
     473            8 :     function getDefaultLibLocation(): string {
     474            8 :         return getDirectoryPath(normalizePath(system.getExecutingFilePath()));
     475            8 :     }
     476            8 : 
     477            8 :     const newLine = getNewLineCharacter(options);
     478            8 :     const realpath = system.realpath && ((path: string) => system.realpath!(path));
     479            8 :     const compilerHost: CompilerHost = {
     480            8 :         getSourceFile: createGetSourceFile(fileName => compilerHost.readFile(fileName), setParentNodes),
     481            8 :         getDefaultLibLocation,
     482            8 :         getDefaultLibFileName: options => combinePaths(getDefaultLibLocation(), getDefaultLibFileName(options)),
     483            8 :         writeFile: createWriteFileMeasuringIO(
     484            8 :             (path, data, writeByteOrderMark) => system.writeFile(path, data, writeByteOrderMark),
     485            8 :             path => (compilerHost.createDirectory || system.createDirectory)(path),
     486            8 :             path => directoryExists(path),
     487            8 :         ),
     488            8 :         getCurrentDirectory: memoize(() => system.getCurrentDirectory()),
     489            8 :         useCaseSensitiveFileNames: () => system.useCaseSensitiveFileNames,
     490            8 :         getCanonicalFileName,
     491            8 :         getNewLine: () => newLine,
     492            8 :         fileExists: fileName => system.fileExists(fileName),
     493            8 :         readFile: fileName => system.readFile(fileName),
     494            8 :         trace: (s: string) => system.write(s + newLine),
     495            8 :         directoryExists: directoryName => system.directoryExists(directoryName),
     496            8 :         getEnvironmentVariable: name => system.getEnvironmentVariable ? system.getEnvironmentVariable(name) : "",
     497            8 :         getDirectories: (path: string) => system.getDirectories(path),
     498            8 :         realpath,
     499            8 :         readDirectory: (path, extensions, include, exclude, depth) => system.readDirectory(path, extensions, include, exclude, depth),
     500            8 :         createDirectory: d => system.createDirectory(d),
     501            8 :         createHash: maybeBind(system, system.createHash),
     502            8 :     };
     503            8 :     return compilerHost;
     504            8 : }

     515            8 : /** @internal */
     516            8 : export function changeCompilerHostLikeToUseCache(
     517            8 :     host: CompilerHostLikeForCache,
     518            8 :     toPath: (fileName: string) => Path,
     519            8 :     getSourceFile?: CompilerHost["getSourceFile"],
     520            8 : ) {
     521            8 :     const originalReadFile = host.readFile;
     522            8 :     const originalFileExists = host.fileExists;
     523            8 :     const originalDirectoryExists = host.directoryExists;
     524            8 :     const originalCreateDirectory = host.createDirectory;
     525            8 :     const originalWriteFile = host.writeFile;
     526            8 :     const readFileCache = new Map<Path, string | false>();
     527            8 :     const fileExistsCache = new Map<Path, boolean>();
     528            8 :     const directoryExistsCache = new Map<Path, boolean>();
     529            8 :     const sourceFileCache = new Map<ResolutionMode, Map<Path, SourceFile>>();
     530            8 : 
     531            8 :     const readFileWithCache = (fileName: string): string | undefined => {
     532            8 :         const key = toPath(fileName);
     533            8 :         const value = readFileCache.get(key);
     534            8 :         if (value !== undefined) return value !== false ? value : undefined;
     535            8 :         return setReadFileCache(key, fileName);
     536            8 :     };
     537            8 :     const setReadFileCache = (key: Path, fileName: string) => {
     538            8 :         const newValue = originalReadFile.call(host, fileName);
     539            8 :         readFileCache.set(key, newValue !== undefined ? newValue : false);
     540            8 :         return newValue;
     541            8 :     };
     542            8 :     host.readFile = fileName => {
     543            8 :         const key = toPath(fileName);
     544            8 :         const value = readFileCache.get(key);
     545            8 :         if (value !== undefined) return value !== false ? value : undefined; // could be .d.ts from output
     546            8 :         // Cache json or buildInfo
     547            8 :         if (!fileExtensionIs(fileName, Extension.Json) && !isBuildInfoFile(fileName)) {
     548            8 :             return originalReadFile.call(host, fileName);
     549            8 :         }
     550            8 : 
     551            8 :         return setReadFileCache(key, fileName);
     552            8 :     };
     553            8 : 
     554            8 :     const getSourceFileWithCache: CompilerHost["getSourceFile"] | undefined = getSourceFile ? (fileName, languageVersionOrOptions, onError, shouldCreateNewSourceFile) => {
     555            8 :         const key = toPath(fileName);
     556            8 :         const impliedNodeFormat: ResolutionMode = typeof languageVersionOrOptions === "object" ? languageVersionOrOptions.impliedNodeFormat : undefined;
     557            8 :         const forImpliedNodeFormat = sourceFileCache.get(impliedNodeFormat);
     558            8 :         const value = forImpliedNodeFormat?.get(key);
     559            8 :         if (value) return value;
     560            8 : 
     561            8 :         const sourceFile = getSourceFile(fileName, languageVersionOrOptions, onError, shouldCreateNewSourceFile);
     562            8 :         if (sourceFile && (isDeclarationFileName(fileName) || fileExtensionIs(fileName, Extension.Json))) {
     563            8 :             sourceFileCache.set(impliedNodeFormat, (forImpliedNodeFormat || new Map()).set(key, sourceFile));
     564            8 :         }
     565            8 :         return sourceFile;
     566            8 :     } : undefined;
     567            8 : 
     568            8 :     // fileExists for any kind of extension
     569            8 :     host.fileExists = fileName => {
     570            8 :         const key = toPath(fileName);
     571            8 :         const value = fileExistsCache.get(key);
     572            8 :         if (value !== undefined) return value;
     573            8 :         const newValue = originalFileExists.call(host, fileName);
     574            8 :         fileExistsCache.set(key, !!newValue);
     575            8 :         return newValue;
     576            8 :     };
     577            8 :     if (originalWriteFile) {
     578            8 :         host.writeFile = (fileName, data, ...rest) => {
     579            8 :             const key = toPath(fileName);
     580            8 :             fileExistsCache.delete(key);
     581            8 : 
     582            8 :             const value = readFileCache.get(key);
     583            8 :             if (value !== undefined && value !== data) {
     584            8 :                 readFileCache.delete(key);
     585            8 :                 sourceFileCache.forEach(map => map.delete(key));
     586            8 :             }
     587            8 :             else if (getSourceFileWithCache) {
     588            8 :                 sourceFileCache.forEach(map => {
     589            8 :                     const sourceFile = map.get(key);
     590            8 :                     if (sourceFile && sourceFile.text !== data) {
     591            8 :                         map.delete(key);
     592            8 :                     }
     593            8 :                 });
     594            8 :             }
     595            8 :             originalWriteFile.call(host, fileName, data, ...rest);
     596            8 :         };
     597            8 :     }
     598            8 : 
     599            8 :     // directoryExists
     600            8 :     if (originalDirectoryExists) {
     601            8 :         host.directoryExists = directory => {
     602            8 :             const key = toPath(directory);
     603            8 :             const value = directoryExistsCache.get(key);
     604            8 :             if (value !== undefined) return value;
     605            8 :             const newValue = originalDirectoryExists.call(host, directory);
     606            8 :             directoryExistsCache.set(key, !!newValue);
     607            8 :             return newValue;
     608            8 :         };
     609            8 : 
     610            8 :         if (originalCreateDirectory) {
     611            8 :             host.createDirectory = directory => {
     612            8 :                 const key = toPath(directory);
     613            8 :                 directoryExistsCache.delete(key);
     614            8 :                 originalCreateDirectory.call(host, directory);
     615            8 :             };
     616            8 :         }
     617            8 :     }
     618            8 : 
     619            8 :     return {
     620            8 :         originalReadFile,
     621            8 :         originalFileExists,
     622            8 :         originalDirectoryExists,
     623            8 :         originalCreateDirectory,
     624            8 :         originalWriteFile,
     625            8 :         getSourceFileWithCache,
     626            8 :         readFileWithCache,
     627            8 :     };
     628            8 : }
     629            8 : 
     630            8 : export function getPreEmitDiagnostics(program: Program, sourceFile?: SourceFile, cancellationToken?: CancellationToken): readonly Diagnostic[];
     631            8 : /** @internal */ export function getPreEmitDiagnostics(program: BuilderProgram, sourceFile?: SourceFile, cancellationToken?: CancellationToken): readonly Diagnostic[]; // eslint-disable-line @typescript-eslint/unified-signatures
     632            8 : export function getPreEmitDiagnostics(program: Program | BuilderProgram, sourceFile?: SourceFile, cancellationToken?: CancellationToken): readonly Diagnostic[] {
     633            8 :     let diagnostics: Diagnostic[] | undefined;
     634            8 :     diagnostics = addRange(diagnostics, program.getConfigFileParsingDiagnostics());
     635            8 :     diagnostics = addRange(diagnostics, program.getOptionsDiagnostics(cancellationToken));

     638            8 :     diagnostics = addRange(diagnostics, program.getSemanticDiagnostics(sourceFile, cancellationToken));

     641            8 :         diagnostics = addRange(diagnostics, program.getDeclarationDiagnostics(sourceFile, cancellationToken));
     642            8 :     }

     662            8 : export function formatDiagnostic(diagnostic: Diagnostic, host: FormatDiagnosticsHost): string {

     664            8 :

     675            8 : /** @internal */
     676            8 : export enum ForegroundColorEscapeSequences {
     677            8 :     Grey = "\u001b[90m",
     678            8 :     Red = "\u001b[91m",
     679            8 :     Yellow = "\u001b[93m",
     680            8 :     Blue = "\u001b[94m",
     681            8 :     Cyan = "\u001b[96m",
     682            8 : }
     683            8 : const gutterStyleSequence = "\u001b[7m";
     684            8 : const gutterSeparator = " ";
     685            8 : const resetEscapeSequence = "\u001b[0m";
     686            8 : const ellipsis = "...";
     687            8 : const halfIndent = "  ";
     688            8 : const indent = "    ";
     689            8 : function getCategoryFormat(category: DiagnosticCategory): ForegroundColorEscapeSequences {
     690            8 :     switch (category) {
     691            8 :         case DiagnosticCategory.Error:
     692            8 :             return ForegroundColorEscapeSequences.Red;
     693            8 :         case DiagnosticCategory.Warning:
     694            8 :             return ForegroundColorEscapeSequences.Yellow;
     695            8 :         case DiagnosticCategory.Suggestion:
     696            8 :             return Debug.fail("Should never get an Info diagnostic on the command line.");
     697            8 :         case DiagnosticCategory.Message:
     698            8 :             return ForegroundColorEscapeSequences.Blue;
     699            8 :     }
     700            8 : }
     701            8 : 
     702            8 : /** @internal */
     703            8 : export function formatColorAndReset(text: string, formatStyle: string) {
     704            8 :     return formatStyle + text + resetEscapeSequence;
     705            8 : }
     706            8 : 
     707            8 : function formatCodeSpan(file: SourceFile, start: number, length: number, indent: string, squiggleColor: ForegroundColorEscapeSequences, host: FormatDiagnosticsHost) {
     708            8 :     const { line: firstLine, character: firstLineChar } = getLineAndCharacterOfPosition(file, start);
     709            8 :     const { line: lastLine, character: lastLineChar } = getLineAndCharacterOfPosition(file, start + length);
     710            8 :     const lastLineInFile = getLineAndCharacterOfPosition(file, file.text.length).line;
     711            8 : 
     712            8 :     const hasMoreThanFiveLines = (lastLine - firstLine) >= 4;
     713            8 :     let gutterWidth = (lastLine + 1 + "").length;
     714            8 :     if (hasMoreThanFiveLines) {
     715            8 :         gutterWidth = Math.max(ellipsis.length, gutterWidth);
     716            8 :     }
     717            8 : 
     718            8 :     let context = "";
     719            8 :     for (let i = firstLine; i <= lastLine; i++) {
     720            8 :         context += host.getNewLine();
     721            8 :         // If the error spans over 5 lines, we'll only show the first 2 and last 2 lines,
     722            8 :         // so we'll skip ahead to the second-to-last line.
     723            8 :         if (hasMoreThanFiveLines && firstLine + 1 < i && i < lastLine - 1) {
     724            8 :             context += indent + formatColorAndReset(ellipsis.padStart(gutterWidth), gutterStyleSequence) + gutterSeparator + host.getNewLine();
     725            8 :             i = lastLine - 1;
     726            8 :         }
     727            8 : 
     728            8 :         const lineStart = getPositionOfLineAndCharacter(file, i, 0);
     729            8 :         const lineEnd = i < lastLineInFile ? getPositionOfLineAndCharacter(file, i + 1, 0) : file.text.length;
     730            8 :         let lineContent = file.text.slice(lineStart, lineEnd);
     731            8 :         lineContent = lineContent.trimEnd(); // trim from end
     732            8 :         lineContent = lineContent.replace(/\t/g, " "); // convert tabs to single spaces
     733            8 : 
     734            8 :         // Output the gutter and the actual contents of the line.
     735            8 :         context += indent + formatColorAndReset((i + 1 + "").padStart(gutterWidth), gutterStyleSequence) + gutterSeparator;
     736            8 :         context += lineContent + host.getNewLine();
     737            8 : 
     738            8 :         // Output the gutter and the error span for the line using tildes.
     739            8 :         context += indent + formatColorAndReset("".padStart(gutterWidth), gutterStyleSequence) + gutterSeparator;
     740            8 :         context += squiggleColor;
     741            8 :         if (i === firstLine) {
     742            8 :             // If we're on the last line, then limit it to the last character of the last line.
     743            8 :             // Otherwise, we'll just squiggle the rest of the line, giving 'slice' no end position.
     744            8 :             const lastCharForLine = i === lastLine ? lastLineChar : undefined;
     745            8 : 
     746            8 :             context += lineContent.slice(0, firstLineChar).replace(/\S/g, " ");
     747            8 :             context += lineContent.slice(firstLineChar, lastCharForLine).replace(/./g, "~");
     748            8 :         }
     749            8 :         else if (i === lastLine) {
     750            8 :             context += lineContent.slice(0, lastLineChar).replace(/./g, "~");
     751            8 :         }
     752            8 :         else {
     753            8 :             // Squiggle the entire line.
     754            8 :             context += lineContent.replace(/./g, "~");
     755            8 :         }
     756            8 :         context += resetEscapeSequence;
     757            8 :     }
     758            8 :     return context;
     759            8 : }
     760            8 : 
     761            8 : /** @internal */
     762            8 : export function formatLocation(file: SourceFile, start: number, host: FormatDiagnosticsHost, color = formatColorAndReset) {
     763            8 :     const { line: firstLine, character: firstLineChar } = getLineAndCharacterOfPosition(file, start); // TODO: GH#18217
     764            8 :     const relativeFileName = host ? convertToRelativePath(file.fileName, host.getCurrentDirectory(), fileName => host.getCanonicalFileName(fileName)) : file.fileName;
     765            8 : 
     766            8 :     let output = "";
     767            8 :     output += color(relativeFileName, ForegroundColorEscapeSequences.Cyan);
     768            8 :     output += ":";
     769            8 :     output += color(`${firstLine + 1}`, ForegroundColorEscapeSequences.Yellow);
     770            8 :     output += ":";
     771            8 :     output += color(`${firstLineChar + 1}`, ForegroundColorEscapeSequences.Yellow);
     772            8 :     return output;
     773            8 : }

     775            8 : export function formatDiagnosticsWithColorAndContext(diagnostics: readonly Diagnostic[], host: FormatDiagnosticsHost): string {
     776            8 :     let output = "";
     777            8 :     for (const diagnostic of diagnostics) {
     778            8 :         if (diagnostic.file) {
     779            8 :             const { file, start } = diagnostic;
     780            8 :             output += formatLocation(file, start!, host); // TODO: GH#18217
     781            8 :             output += " - ";
     782            8 :         }
     783            8 : 
     784            8 :         output += formatColorAndReset(diagnosticCategoryName(diagnostic), getCategoryFormat(diagnostic.category));
     785            8 :         output += formatColorAndReset(` TS${diagnostic.code}: `, ForegroundColorEscapeSequences.Grey);

     791            8 :         }

     799            8 :                 }

     802            8 :             }
     803            8 :         }

     805            8 :     }
     806            8 :     return output;
     807            8 : }
     808            8 : 
     809            8 : export function flattenDiagnosticMessageText(diag: string | DiagnosticMessageChain | undefined, newLine: string, indent = 0): string {
     810            8 :     if (isString(diag)) {
     811            8 :         return diag;
     812            8 :     }
     813            8 :     else if (diag === undefined) {
     814            8 :         return "";
     815            8 :     }
     816            8 :     let result = "";
     817            8 :     if (indent) {
     818            8 :         result += newLine;
     819            8 : 
     820            8 :         for (let i = 0; i < indent; i++) {
     821            8 :             result += "  ";
     822            8 :         }
     823            8 :     }
     824            8 :     result += diag.messageText;
     825            8 :     indent++;
     826            8 :     if (diag.next) {
     827            8 :         for (const kid of diag.next) {
     828            8 :             result += flattenDiagnosticMessageText(kid, newLine, indent);
     829            8 :         }
     830            8 :     }
     831            8 :     return result;
     832            8 : }

     849            8 : /**

     856            8 : 
     857            8 : /**
     858            8 :  * Use `program.getModeForResolutionAtIndex`, which retrieves the correct `compilerOptions`, instead of this function whenever possible.
     859            8 :  * Calculates the final resolution mode for an import at some index within a file's `imports` list. This is the resolution mode
     860            8 :  * explicitly provided via import attributes, if present, or the syntax the usage would have if emitted to JavaScript. In
     861            8 :  * `--module node16` or `nodenext`, this may depend on the file's `impliedNodeFormat`. In `--module preserve`, it depends only on the
     862            8 :  * input syntax of the reference. In other `module` modes, when overriding import attributes are not provided, this function returns
     863            8 :  * `undefined`, as the result would have no impact on module resolution, emit, or type checking.
     864            8 :  * @param file File to fetch the resolution mode within
     865            8 :  * @param index Index into the file's complete resolution list to get the resolution of - this is a concatenation of the file's imports and module augmentations
     866            8 :  * @param compilerOptions The compiler options for the program that owns the file. If the file belongs to a referenced project, the compiler options
     867            8 :  * should be the options of the referenced project, not the referencing project.
     868            8 :  */
     869            8 : export function getModeForResolutionAtIndex(file: SourceFile, index: number, compilerOptions: CompilerOptions): ResolutionMode;
     870            8 : /** @internal */
     871            8 : // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/unified-signatures
     872            8 : export function getModeForResolutionAtIndex(file: SourceFileImportsList, index: number, compilerOptions: CompilerOptions): ResolutionMode;
     873            8 : export function getModeForResolutionAtIndex(file: SourceFileImportsList, index: number, compilerOptions?: CompilerOptions): ResolutionMode {
     874            8 :     // we ensure all elements of file.imports and file.moduleAugmentations have the relevant parent pointers set during program setup,
     875            8 :     // so it's safe to use them even pre-bind
     876            8 :     return getModeForUsageLocationWorker(file, getModuleNameStringLiteralAt(file, index), compilerOptions);
     877            8 : }

     879            8 : /** @internal */
     880            8 : export function isExclusivelyTypeOnlyImportOrExport(decl: ImportDeclaration | ExportDeclaration | JSDocImportTag) {
     881            8 :     if (isExportDeclaration(decl)) {
     882            8 :         return decl.isTypeOnly;
     883            8 :     }
     884            8 :     if (decl.importClause?.isTypeOnly) {
     885            8 :         return true;
     886            8 :     }
     887            8 :     return false;
     888            8 : }
     889            8 : 
     890            8 : /**
     891            8 :  * Use `program.getModeForUsageLocation`, which retrieves the correct `compilerOptions`, instead of this function whenever possible.
     892            8 :  * Calculates the final resolution mode for a given module reference node. This function only returns a result when module resolution
     893            8 :  * settings allow differing resolution between ESM imports and CJS requires, or when a mode is explicitly provided via import attributes,
     894            8 :  * which cause an `import` or `require` condition to be used during resolution regardless of module resolution settings. In absence of
     895            8 :  * overriding attributes, and in modes that support differing resolution, the result indicates the syntax the usage would emit to JavaScript.
     896            8 :  * Some examples:
     897            8 :  *
     898            8 :  * ```ts
     899            8 :  * // tsc foo.mts --module nodenext
     900            8 :  * import {} from "mod";
     901            8 :  * // Result: ESNext - the import emits as ESM due to `impliedNodeFormat` set by .mts file extension
     902            8 :  *
     903            8 :  * // tsc foo.cts --module nodenext
     904            8 :  * import {} from "mod";
     905            8 :  * // Result: CommonJS - the import emits as CJS due to `impliedNodeFormat` set by .cts file extension
     906            8 :  *
     907            8 :  * // tsc foo.ts --module preserve --moduleResolution bundler
     908            8 :  * import {} from "mod";
     909            8 :  * // Result: ESNext - the import emits as ESM due to `--module preserve` and `--moduleResolution bundler`
     910            8 :  * // supports conditional imports/exports
     911            8 :  *
     912            8 :  * // tsc foo.ts --module preserve --moduleResolution node10
     913            8 :  * import {} from "mod";
     914            8 :  * // Result: undefined - the import emits as ESM due to `--module preserve`, but `--moduleResolution node10`
     915            8 :  * // does not support conditional imports/exports
     916            8 :  *
     917            8 :  * // tsc foo.ts --module commonjs --moduleResolution node10
     918            8 :  * import type {} from "mod" with { "resolution-mode": "import" };
     919            8 :  * // Result: ESNext - conditional imports/exports always supported with "resolution-mode" attribute
     920            8 :  * ```
     921            8 :  *
     922            8 :  * @param file The file the import or import-like reference is contained within
     923            8 :  * @param usage The module reference string
     924            8 :  * @param compilerOptions The compiler options for the program that owns the file. If the file belongs to a referenced project, the compiler options
     925            8 :  * should be the options of the referenced project, not the referencing project.
     926            8 :  * @returns The final resolution mode of the import
     927            8 :  */
     928            8 : export function getModeForUsageLocation(file: SourceFile, usage: StringLiteralLike, compilerOptions: CompilerOptions) {
     929            8 :     return getModeForUsageLocationWorker(file, usage, compilerOptions);
     930            8 : }
     931            8 : 
     932            8 : function getModeForUsageLocationWorker(file: Pick<SourceFile, "fileName" | "impliedNodeFormat" | "packageJsonScope">, usage: StringLiteralLike, compilerOptions?: CompilerOptions) {
     933            8 :     if ((isImportDeclaration(usage.parent) || isExportDeclaration(usage.parent))) {
     934            8 :         const isTypeOnly = isExclusivelyTypeOnlyImportOrExport(usage.parent);
     935            8 :         if (isTypeOnly) {
     936            8 :             const override = getResolutionModeOverride(usage.parent.attributes);
     937            8 :             if (override) {
     938            8 :                 return override;
     939            8 :             }
     940            8 :         }
     941            8 :     }
     942            8 :     if (usage.parent.parent && isImportTypeNode(usage.parent.parent)) {
     943            8 :         const override = getResolutionModeOverride(usage.parent.parent.attributes);
     944            8 :         if (override) {
     945            8 :             return override;
     946            8 :         }
     947            8 :     }
     948            8 : 
     949            8 :     if (compilerOptions && importSyntaxAffectsModuleResolution(compilerOptions)) {
     950            8 :         return getEmitSyntaxForUsageLocationWorker(file, usage, compilerOptions);
     951            8 :     }
     952            8 : }
     953            8 : 
     954            8 : function getEmitSyntaxForUsageLocationWorker(file: Pick<SourceFile, "fileName" | "impliedNodeFormat" | "packageJsonScope">, usage: StringLiteralLike, compilerOptions?: CompilerOptions): ResolutionMode {
     955            8 :     if (!compilerOptions) {
     956            8 :         // This should always be provided, but we try to fail somewhat
     957            8 :         // gracefully to allow projects like ts-node time to update.
     958            8 :         return undefined;
     959            8 :     }
     960            8 :     const exprParentParent = walkUpParenthesizedExpressions(usage.parent)?.parent;
     961            8 :     if (exprParentParent && isImportEqualsDeclaration(exprParentParent) || isRequireCall(usage.parent, /*requireStringLiteralLikeArgument*/ false)) {
     962            8 :         return ModuleKind.CommonJS;
     963            8 :     }
     964            8 :     if (isImportCall(walkUpParenthesizedExpressions(usage.parent))) {
     965            8 :         return shouldTransformImportCallWorker(file, compilerOptions) ? ModuleKind.CommonJS : ModuleKind.ESNext;
     966            8 :     }
     967            8 :     // If we're in --module preserve on an input file, we know that an import
     968            8 :     // is an import. But if this is a declaration file, we'd prefer to use the
     969            8 :     // impliedNodeFormat. Since we want things to be consistent between the two,
     970            8 :     // we need to issue errors when the user writes ESM syntax in a definitely-CJS
     971            8 :     // file, until/unless declaration emit can indicate a true ESM import. On the
     972            8 :     // other hand, writing CJS syntax in a definitely-ESM file is fine, since declaration
     973            8 :     // emit preserves the CJS syntax.
     974            8 :     const fileEmitMode = getEmitModuleFormatOfFileWorker(file, compilerOptions);
     975            8 :     return fileEmitMode === ModuleKind.CommonJS ? ModuleKind.CommonJS :
     976            8 :         emitModuleKindIsNonNodeESM(fileEmitMode) || fileEmitMode === ModuleKind.Preserve ? ModuleKind.ESNext :
     977            8 :         undefined;
     978            8 : }
     979            8 : 
     980            8 : /** @internal */
     981            8 : export function getResolutionModeOverride(node: ImportAttributes | undefined, grammarErrorOnNode?: (node: Node, diagnostic: DiagnosticMessage) => void) {
     982            8 :     if (!node) return undefined;
     983            8 :     if (length(node.elements) !== 1) {
     984            8 :         grammarErrorOnNode?.(
     985            8 :             node,
     986            8 :             node.token === SyntaxKind.WithKeyword
     987            8 :                 ? Diagnostics.Type_import_attributes_should_have_exactly_one_key_resolution_mode_with_value_import_or_require
     988            8 :                 : Diagnostics.Type_import_assertions_should_have_exactly_one_key_resolution_mode_with_value_import_or_require,
     989            8 :         );
     990            8 :         return undefined;
     991            8 :     }
     992            8 :     const elem = node.elements[0];

    1000            8 :         );

    1094            8 : export function loadWithModeAwareCache<Entry, SourceFile, ResolutionCache, Resolution>(
    1095            8 :     entries: readonly Entry[],
    1096            8 :     containingFile: string,
    1097            8 :     redirectedReference: ResolvedProjectReference | undefined,
    1098            8 :     options: CompilerOptions,
    1099            8 :     containingSourceFile: SourceFile,
    1100            8 :     host: ModuleResolutionHost,
    1101            8 :     resolutionCache: ResolutionCache | undefined,
    1102            8 :     createLoader: (
    1103            8 :         containingFile: string,
    1104            8 :         redirectedReference: ResolvedProjectReference | undefined,
    1105            8 :         options: CompilerOptions,
    1106            8 :         host: ModuleResolutionHost,
    1107            8 :         resolutionCache: ResolutionCache | undefined,
    1108            8 :     ) => ResolutionLoader<Entry, Resolution, SourceFile>,
    1109            8 : ): readonly Resolution[] {
    1110            8 :     if (entries.length === 0) return emptyArray;
    1111            8 :     const resolutions: Resolution[] = [];
    1112            8 :     const cache = new Map<ModeAwareCacheKey, Resolution>();
    1113            8 :     const loader = createLoader(containingFile, redirectedReference, options, host, resolutionCache);
    1114            8 :     for (const entry of entries) {
    1115            8 :         const name = loader.nameAndMode.getName(entry);
    1116            8 :         const mode = loader.nameAndMode.getMode(entry, containingSourceFile, redirectedReference?.commandLine.options || options);
    1117            8 :         const key = createModeAwareCacheKey(name, mode);
    1118            8 :         let result = cache.get(key);
    1119            8 :         if (!result) {
    1120            8 :             cache.set(key, result = loader.resolve(name, mode));
    1121            8 :         }
    1122            8 :         resolutions.push(result);
    1123            8 :     }
    1124            8 :     return resolutions;
    1125            8 : }

    1127            8 : /** @internal */
    1128            8 : export function forEachResolvedProjectReference<T>(
    1129            8 :     resolvedProjectReferences: readonly (ResolvedProjectReference | undefined)[] | undefined,
    1130            8 :     cb: (resolvedProjectReference: ResolvedProjectReference, parent: ResolvedProjectReference | undefined) => T | undefined,
    1131            8 : ): T | undefined {
    1132            8 :     return forEachProjectReference(/*projectReferences*/ undefined, resolvedProjectReferences, (resolvedRef, parent) => resolvedRef && cb(resolvedRef, parent));
    1133            8 : }
    1134            8 : 
    1135            8 : function forEachProjectReference<T>(
    1136            8 :     projectReferences: readonly ProjectReference[] | undefined,
    1137            8 :     resolvedProjectReferences: readonly (ResolvedProjectReference | undefined)[] | undefined,
    1138            8 :     cbResolvedRef: (resolvedRef: ResolvedProjectReference | undefined, parent: ResolvedProjectReference | undefined, index: number) => T | undefined,
    1139            8 :     cbRef?: (projectReferences: readonly ProjectReference[] | undefined, parent: ResolvedProjectReference | undefined) => T | undefined,
    1140            8 : ): T | undefined {
    1141            8 :     let seenResolvedRefs: Set<Path> | undefined;
    1142            8 : 
    1143            8 :     return worker(projectReferences, resolvedProjectReferences, /*parent*/ undefined);
    1144            8 : 
    1145            8 :     function worker(
    1146            8 :         projectReferences: readonly ProjectReference[] | undefined,
    1147            8 :         resolvedProjectReferences: readonly (ResolvedProjectReference | undefined)[] | undefined,
    1148            8 :         parent: ResolvedProjectReference | undefined,
    1149            8 :     ): T | undefined {
    1150            8 :         // Visit project references first
    1151            8 :         if (cbRef) {
    1152            8 :             const result = cbRef(projectReferences, parent);
    1153            8 :             if (result) return result;
    1154            8 :         }
    1155            8 : 
    1156            8 :         return forEach(resolvedProjectReferences, (resolvedRef, index) => {
    1157            8 :             if (resolvedRef && seenResolvedRefs?.has(resolvedRef.sourceFile.path)) {
    1158            8 :                 // ignore recursives
    1159            8 :                 return undefined;
    1160            8 :             }
    1161            8 : 
    1162            8 :             const result = cbResolvedRef(resolvedRef, parent, index);
    1163            8 :             if (result || !resolvedRef) return result;
    1164            8 : 
    1165            8 :             (seenResolvedRefs ||= new Set()).add(resolvedRef.sourceFile.path);
    1166            8 :             return worker(resolvedRef.commandLine.projectReferences, resolvedRef.references, resolvedRef);
    1167            8 :         });
    1168            8 :     }
    1169            8 : }

    1181            8 : export function getLibraryNameFromLibFileName(libFileName: string) {
    1182            8 :     // Support resolving to lib.dom.d.ts -> @typescript/lib-dom, and
    1183            8 :     //                      lib.dom.iterable.d.ts -> @typescript/lib-dom/iterable
    1184            8 :     //                      lib.es2015.symbol.wellknown.d.ts -> @typescript/lib-es2015/symbol-wellknown
    1185            8 :     const components = libFileName.split(".");
    1186            8 :     let path = components[1];
    1187            8 :     let i = 2;
    1188            8 :     while (components[i] && components[i] !== "d") {
    1189            8 :         path += (i === 2 ? "/" : "-") + components[i];
    1190            8 :         i++;
    1191            8 :     }
    1192            8 :     return "@typescript/lib-" + path;
    1193            8 : }

    1242            8 : /** @internal */
    1243            8 : export function getReferencedFileLocation(program: Program, ref: ReferencedFile): ReferenceFileLocation | SyntheticReferenceFileLocation {
    1244            8 :     const file = Debug.checkDefined(program.getSourceFileByPath(ref.file));
    1245            8 :     const { kind, index } = ref;
    1246            8 :     let pos: number | undefined, end: number | undefined, packageId: PackageId | undefined;
    1247            8 :     switch (kind) {
    1248            8 :         case FileIncludeKind.Import:
    1249            8 :             const importLiteral = getModuleNameStringLiteralAt(file, index);
    1250            8 :             packageId = program.getResolvedModuleFromModuleSpecifier(importLiteral, file)?.resolvedModule?.packageId;
    1251            8 :             if (importLiteral.pos === -1) return { file, packageId, text: importLiteral.text };
    1252            8 :             pos = skipTrivia(file.text, importLiteral.pos);
    1253            8 :             end = importLiteral.end;
    1254            8 :             break;
    1255            8 :         case FileIncludeKind.ReferenceFile:
    1256            8 :             ({ pos, end } = file.referencedFiles[index]);
    1257            8 :             break;
    1258            8 :         case FileIncludeKind.TypeReferenceDirective:
    1259            8 :             ({ pos, end } = file.typeReferenceDirectives[index]);
    1260            8 :             packageId = program.getResolvedTypeReferenceDirectiveFromTypeReferenceDirective(file.typeReferenceDirectives[index], file)?.resolvedTypeReferenceDirective?.packageId;
    1261            8 :             break;
    1262            8 :         case FileIncludeKind.LibReferenceDirective:
    1263            8 :             ({ pos, end } = file.libReferenceDirectives[index]);
    1264            8 :             break;
    1265            8 :         default:
    1266            8 :             return Debug.assertNever(kind);
    1267            8 :     }
    1268            8 :     return { file, pos, end, packageId };
    1269            8 : }

    1271            8 : /**
    1272            8 :  * Determines if program structure is upto date or needs to be recreated
    1273            8 :  *
    1274            8 :  * @internal
    1275            8 :  */
    1276            8 : export function isProgramUptoDate(
    1277            8 :     program: Program | undefined,
    1278            8 :     rootFileNames: string[],
    1279            8 :     newOptions: CompilerOptions,
    1280            8 :     getSourceVersion: (path: Path, fileName: string) => string | undefined,
    1281            8 :     fileExists: (fileName: string) => boolean,
    1282            8 :     hasInvalidatedResolutions: HasInvalidatedResolutions,
    1283            8 :     hasInvalidatedLibResolutions: HasInvalidatedLibResolutions,
    1284            8 :     hasChangedAutomaticTypeDirectiveNames: HasChangedAutomaticTypeDirectiveNames | undefined,
    1285            8 :     getParsedCommandLine: (fileName: string) => ParsedCommandLine | undefined,
    1286            8 :     projectReferences: readonly ProjectReference[] | undefined,
    1287            8 : ): boolean {
    1288            8 :     // If we haven't created a program yet or have changed automatic type directives, then it is not up-to-date
    1289            8 :     if (!program || hasChangedAutomaticTypeDirectiveNames?.()) return false;
    1290            8 : 
    1291            8 :     // If root file names don't match
    1292            8 :     if (!arrayIsEqualTo(program.getRootFileNames(), rootFileNames)) return false;
    1293            8 : 
    1294            8 :     let seenResolvedRefs: ResolvedProjectReference[] | undefined;
    1295            8 : 
    1296            8 :     // If project references don't match
    1297            8 :     if (!arrayIsEqualTo(program.getProjectReferences(), projectReferences, projectReferenceUptoDate)) return false;
    1298            8 : 
    1299            8 :     // If any file is not up-to-date, then the whole program is not up-to-date
    1300            8 :     if (program.getSourceFiles().some(sourceFileNotUptoDate)) return false;
    1301            8 : 
    1302            8 :     // If any of the missing file paths are now created
    1303            8 :     const missingPaths = program.getMissingFilePaths();
    1304            8 :     if (missingPaths && forEachEntry(missingPaths, fileExists)) return false;
    1305            8 : 
    1306            8 :     const currentOptions = program.getCompilerOptions();
    1307            8 :     // If the compilation settings do no match, then the program is not up-to-date
    1308            8 :     if (!compareDataObjects(currentOptions, newOptions)) return false;
    1309            8 : 
    1310            8 :     // If library resolution is invalidated, then the program is not up-to-date
    1311            8 :     if (program.resolvedLibReferences && forEachEntry(program.resolvedLibReferences, (_value, libFileName) => hasInvalidatedLibResolutions(libFileName))) return false;
    1312            8 : 
    1313            8 :     // If everything matches but the text of config file is changed,
    1314            8 :     // error locations can change for program options, so update the program
    1315            8 :     if (currentOptions.configFile && newOptions.configFile) return currentOptions.configFile.text === newOptions.configFile.text;
    1316            8 : 
    1317            8 :     return true;
    1318            8 : 
    1319            8 :     function sourceFileNotUptoDate(sourceFile: SourceFile) {
    1320            8 :         return !sourceFileVersionUptoDate(sourceFile) ||
    1321            8 :             hasInvalidatedResolutions(sourceFile.path);
    1322            8 :     }
    1323            8 : 
    1324            8 :     function sourceFileVersionUptoDate(sourceFile: SourceFile) {
    1325            8 :         return sourceFile.version === getSourceVersion(sourceFile.resolvedPath, sourceFile.fileName);
    1326            8 :     }
    1327            8 : 
    1328            8 :     function projectReferenceUptoDate(oldRef: ProjectReference, newRef: ProjectReference, index: number) {
    1329            8 :         return projectReferenceIsEqualTo(oldRef, newRef) &&
    1330            8 :             resolvedProjectReferenceUptoDate(program!.getResolvedProjectReferences()![index], oldRef);
    1331            8 :     }
    1332            8 : 
    1333            8 :     function resolvedProjectReferenceUptoDate(oldResolvedRef: ResolvedProjectReference | undefined, oldRef: ProjectReference): boolean {
    1334            8 :         if (oldResolvedRef) {
    1335            8 :             // Assume true
    1336            8 :             if (contains(seenResolvedRefs, oldResolvedRef)) return true;
    1337            8 : 
    1338            8 :             const refPath = resolveProjectReferencePath(oldRef);
    1339            8 :             const newParsedCommandLine = getParsedCommandLine(refPath);
    1340            8 : 
    1341            8 :             // Check if config file exists
    1342            8 :             if (!newParsedCommandLine) return false;
    1343            8 : 
    1344            8 :             // If change in source file
    1345            8 :             if (oldResolvedRef.commandLine.options.configFile !== newParsedCommandLine.options.configFile) return false;
    1346            8 : 
    1347            8 :             // check file names
    1348            8 :             if (!arrayIsEqualTo(oldResolvedRef.commandLine.fileNames, newParsedCommandLine.fileNames)) return false;
    1349            8 : 
    1350            8 :             // Add to seen before checking the referenced paths of this config file
    1351            8 :             (seenResolvedRefs || (seenResolvedRefs = [])).push(oldResolvedRef);
    1352            8 : 
    1353            8 :             // If child project references are upto date, this project reference is uptodate
    1354            8 :             return !forEach(oldResolvedRef.references, (childResolvedRef, index) => !resolvedProjectReferenceUptoDate(childResolvedRef, oldResolvedRef.commandLine.projectReferences![index]));
    1355            8 :         }
    1356            8 : 
    1357            8 :         // In old program, not able to resolve project reference path,
    1358            8 :         // so if config file doesnt exist, it is uptodate.
    1359            8 :         const refPath = resolveProjectReferencePath(oldRef);
    1360            8 :         return !getParsedCommandLine(refPath);
    1361            8 :     }
    1362            8 : }

    1370            8 : /**
    1371            8 :  * A function for determining if a given file is esm or cjs format, assuming modern node module resolution rules, as configured by the
    1372            8 :  * `options` parameter.
    1373            8 :  *
    1374            8 :  * @param fileName The file name to check the format of (it need not exist on disk)
    1375            8 :  * @param [packageJsonInfoCache] A cache for package file lookups - it's best to have a cache when this function is called often
    1376            8 :  * @param host The ModuleResolutionHost which can perform the filesystem lookups for package json data
    1377            8 :  * @param options The compiler options to perform the analysis under - relevant options are `moduleResolution` and `traceResolution`
    1378            8 :  * @returns `undefined` if the path has no relevant implied format, `ModuleKind.ESNext` for esm format, and `ModuleKind.CommonJS` for cjs format
    1379            8 :  */
    1380            8 : export function getImpliedNodeFormatForFile(fileName: string, packageJsonInfoCache: PackageJsonInfoCache | undefined, host: ModuleResolutionHost, options: CompilerOptions): ResolutionMode {
    1381            8 :     const result = getImpliedNodeFormatForFileWorker(fileName, packageJsonInfoCache, host, options);
    1382            8 :     return typeof result === "object" ? result.impliedNodeFormat : result;
    1383            8 : }
    1384            8 : 
    1385            8 : /** @internal */
    1386            8 : export function getImpliedNodeFormatForFileWorker(
    1387            8 :     fileName: string,
    1388            8 :     packageJsonInfoCache: PackageJsonInfoCache | undefined,
    1389            8 :     host: ModuleResolutionHost,
    1390            8 :     options: CompilerOptions,
    1391            8 : ) {
    1392            8 :     return fileExtensionIsOneOf(fileName, [Extension.Dmts, Extension.Mts, Extension.Mjs]) ? ModuleKind.ESNext :
    1393            8 :         fileExtensionIsOneOf(fileName, [Extension.Dcts, Extension.Cts, Extension.Cjs]) ? ModuleKind.CommonJS :
    1394            8 :         fileExtensionIsOneOf(fileName, [Extension.Dts, Extension.Ts, Extension.Tsx, Extension.Js, Extension.Jsx]) ? lookupFromPackageJson() :
    1395            8 :         undefined; // other extensions, like `json` or `tsbuildinfo`, are set as `undefined` here but they should never be fed through the transformer pipeline
    1396            8 : 
    1397            8 :     function lookupFromPackageJson(): Partial<CreateSourceFileOptions> {
    1398            8 :         const state = getTemporaryModuleResolutionState(packageJsonInfoCache, host, options);
    1399            8 :         const packageJsonLocations: string[] = [];
    1400            8 :         state.failedLookupLocations = packageJsonLocations;
    1401            8 :         state.affectingLocations = packageJsonLocations;
    1402            8 :         const packageJsonScope = getPackageScopeForPath(fileName, state);
    1403            8 :         const impliedNodeFormat = packageJsonScope?.contents.packageJsonContent.type === "module" ? ModuleKind.ESNext : ModuleKind.CommonJS;
    1404            8 :         return { impliedNodeFormat, packageJsonLocations, packageJsonScope };
    1405            8 :     }
    1406            8 : }

    1542            8 :  * Creating a program proceeds from a set of root files, expanding the set of inputs by following imports and

    2180            8 :         performance.mark("afterResolveTypeReference");

    2182            8 :         tracing?.pop();
    2183            8 :         return result;
    2184            8 :     }

    2186            8 :     function getRedirectReferenceForResolution(file: SourceFile) {
    2187            8 :         const redirect = getResolvedProjectReferenceToRedirect(file.originalFileName);
    2188            8 :         if (redirect || !isDeclarationFileName(file.originalFileName)) return redirect;
    2189            8 : 
    2190            8 :         // The originalFileName could not be actual source file name if file found was d.ts from referecned project
    2191            8 :         // So in this case try to look up if this is output from referenced project, if it is use the redirected project in that case
    2192            8 :         const resultFromDts = getRedirectReferenceForResolutionFromSourceOfProject(file.path);
    2193            8 :         if (resultFromDts) return resultFromDts;
    2194            8 : 
    2195            8 :         // If preserveSymlinks is true, module resolution wont jump the symlink
    2196            8 :         // but the resolved real path may be the .d.ts from project reference
    2197            8 :         // Note:: Currently we try the real path only if the
    2198            8 :         // file is from node_modules to avoid having to run real path on all file paths
    2199            8 :         if (!host.realpath || !options.preserveSymlinks || !file.originalFileName.includes(nodeModulesPathPart)) return undefined;
    2200            8 :         const realDeclarationPath = toPath(host.realpath(file.originalFileName));
    2201            8 :         return realDeclarationPath === file.path ? undefined : getRedirectReferenceForResolutionFromSourceOfProject(realDeclarationPath);
    2202            8 :     }

    2204            8 :     function getRedirectReferenceForResolutionFromSourceOfProject(filePath: Path) {
    2205            8 :         const source = getSourceOfProjectReferenceRedirect(filePath);
    2206            8 :         if (isString(source)) return getResolvedProjectReferenceToRedirect(source);
    2207            8 :         if (!source) return undefined;
    2208            8 :         // Output of .d.ts file so return resolved ref that matches the out file name
    2209            8 :         return forEachResolvedProjectReference(resolvedRef => {
    2210            8 :             const out = resolvedRef.commandLine.options.outFile;
    2211            8 :             if (!out) return undefined;
    2212            8 :             return toPath(out) === filePath ? resolvedRef : undefined;
    2213            8 :         });
    2214            8 :     }

    2220            8 :     function getDefaultLibFilePriority(a: SourceFile) {
    2221            8 :         if (containsPath(defaultLibraryPath, a.fileName, /*ignoreCase*/ false)) {
    2222            8 :             const basename = getBaseFileName(a.fileName);
    2223            8 :             if (basename === "lib.d.ts" || basename === "lib.es6.d.ts") return 0;
    2224            8 :             const name = removeSuffix(removePrefix(basename, "lib."), ".d.ts");
    2225            8 :             const index = libs.indexOf(name);
    2226            8 :             if (index !== -1) return index + 1;
    2227            8 :         }
    2228            8 :         return libs.length + 2;

    2263            8 :     function resolveModuleNamesReusingOldState(moduleNames: readonly StringLiteralLike[], file: SourceFile): readonly ResolvedModuleWithFailedLookupLocations[] {
    2264            8 :         if (structureIsReused === StructureIsReused.Not && !file.ambientModuleNames.length) {
    2265            8 :             // If the old program state does not permit reusing resolutions and `file` does not contain locally defined ambient modules,
    2266            8 :             // the best we can do is fallback to the default logic.
    2267            8 :             return resolveModuleNamesWorker(moduleNames, file, /*reusedNames*/ undefined);
    2268            8 :         }
    2269            8 : 
    2270            8 :         // At this point, we know at least one of the following hold:
    2271            8 :         // - file has local declarations for ambient modules
    2272            8 :         // - old program state is available
    2273            8 :         // With this information, we can infer some module resolutions without performing resolution.
    2274            8 : 
    2275            8 :         /** An ordered list of module names for which we cannot recover the resolution. */
    2276            8 :         let unknownModuleNames: StringLiteralLike[] | undefined;
    2277            8 :         /**
    2278            8 :          * The indexing of elements in this list matches that of `moduleNames`.
    2279            8 :          *
    2280            8 :          * Before combining results, result[i] is in one of the following states:
    2281            8 :          * * undefined: needs to be recomputed,
    2282            8 :          * * predictedToResolveToAmbientModuleMarker: known to be an ambient module.
    2283            8 :          * Needs to be reset to undefined before returning,
    2284            8 :          * * ResolvedModuleFull instance: can be reused.
    2285            8 :          */
    2286            8 :         let result: ResolvedModuleWithFailedLookupLocations[] | undefined;
    2287            8 :         let reusedNames: StringLiteralLike[] | undefined;
    2288            8 :         /** A transient placeholder used to mark predicted resolution in the result list. */
    2289            8 :         const predictedToResolveToAmbientModuleMarker: ResolvedModuleWithFailedLookupLocations = emptyResolution;
    2290            8 :         const oldSourceFile = oldProgram && oldProgram.getSourceFile(file.fileName);
    2291            8 : 
    2292            8 :         for (let i = 0; i < moduleNames.length; i++) {
    2293            8 :             const moduleName = moduleNames[i];
    2294            8 :             // If the source file is unchanged and doesnt have invalidated resolution, reuse the module resolutions
    2295            8 :             if (file === oldSourceFile && !hasInvalidatedResolutions(file.path)) {
    2296            8 :                 const oldResolution = oldProgram?.getResolvedModule(file, moduleName.text, getModeForUsageLocation(file, moduleName));
    2297            8 :                 if (oldResolution?.resolvedModule) {
    2298            8 :                     if (isTraceEnabled(options, host)) {
    2299            8 :                         trace(
    2300            8 :                             host,
    2301            8 :                             oldResolution.resolvedModule.packageId ?
    2302            8 :                                 Diagnostics.Reusing_resolution_of_module_0_from_1_of_old_program_it_was_successfully_resolved_to_2_with_Package_ID_3 :
    2303            8 :                                 Diagnostics.Reusing_resolution_of_module_0_from_1_of_old_program_it_was_successfully_resolved_to_2,
    2304            8 :                             moduleName.text,
    2305            8 :                             getNormalizedAbsolutePath(file.originalFileName, currentDirectory),
    2306            8 :                             oldResolution.resolvedModule.resolvedFileName,
    2307            8 :                             oldResolution.resolvedModule.packageId && packageIdToString(oldResolution.resolvedModule.packageId),
    2308            8 :                         );
    2309            8 :                     }
    2310            8 :                     (result ??= new Array(moduleNames.length))[i] = oldResolution;
    2311            8 :                     (reusedNames ??= []).push(moduleName);
    2312            8 :                     continue;
    2313            8 :                 }
    2314            8 :             }
    2315            8 :             // We know moduleName resolves to an ambient module provided that moduleName:
    2316            8 :             // - is in the list of ambient modules locally declared in the current source file.
    2317            8 :             // - resolved to an ambient module in the old program whose declaration is in an unmodified file
    2318            8 :             //   (so the same module declaration will land in the new program)
    2319            8 :             let resolvesToAmbientModuleInNonModifiedFile = false;
    2320            8 :             if (contains(file.ambientModuleNames, moduleName.text)) {
    2321            8 :                 resolvesToAmbientModuleInNonModifiedFile = true;
    2322            8 :                 if (isTraceEnabled(options, host)) {
    2323            8 :                     trace(host, Diagnostics.Module_0_was_resolved_as_locally_declared_ambient_module_in_file_1, moduleName.text, getNormalizedAbsolutePath(file.originalFileName, currentDirectory));
    2324            8 :                 }
    2325            8 :             }
    2326            8 :             else {
    2327            8 :                 resolvesToAmbientModuleInNonModifiedFile = moduleNameResolvesToAmbientModuleInNonModifiedFile(moduleName);
    2328            8 :             }
    2329            8 : 
    2330            8 :             if (resolvesToAmbientModuleInNonModifiedFile) {
    2331            8 :                 (result || (result = new Array(moduleNames.length)))[i] = predictedToResolveToAmbientModuleMarker;
    2332            8 :             }
    2333            8 :             else {
    2334            8 :                 // Resolution failed in the old program, or resolved to an ambient module for which we can't reuse the result.
    2335            8 :                 (unknownModuleNames ??= []).push(moduleName);
    2336            8 :             }
    2337            8 :         }
    2338            8 : 
    2339            8 :         const resolutions = unknownModuleNames && unknownModuleNames.length
    2340            8 :             ? resolveModuleNamesWorker(unknownModuleNames, file, reusedNames)
    2341            8 :             : emptyArray;
    2342            8 : 
    2343            8 :         // Combine results of resolutions and predicted results
    2344            8 :         if (!result) {
    2345            8 :             // There were no unresolved/ambient resolutions.
    2346            8 :             Debug.assert(resolutions.length === moduleNames.length);
    2347            8 :             return resolutions;
    2348            8 :         }
    2349            8 : 
    2350            8 :         let j = 0;
    2351            8 :         for (let i = 0; i < result.length; i++) {
    2352            8 :             if (!result[i]) {
    2353            8 :                 result[i] = resolutions[j];
    2354            8 :                 j++;
    2355            8 :             }
    2356            8 :         }
    2357            8 :         Debug.assert(j === resolutions.length);
    2358            8 : 
    2359            8 :         return result;
    2360            8 : 
    2361            8 :         // If we change our policy of rechecking failed lookups on each program create,
    2362            8 :         // we should adjust the value returned here.
    2363            8 :         function moduleNameResolvesToAmbientModuleInNonModifiedFile(moduleName: StringLiteralLike): boolean {
    2364            8 :             const resolutionToFile = oldProgram?.getResolvedModule(file, moduleName.text, getModeForUsageLocation(file, moduleName))?.resolvedModule;
    2365            8 :             const resolvedFile = resolutionToFile && oldProgram!.getSourceFile(resolutionToFile.resolvedFileName);
    2366            8 :             if (resolutionToFile && resolvedFile) {
    2367            8 :                 // In the old program, we resolved to an ambient module that was in the same
    2368            8 :                 //   place as we expected to find an actual module file.
    2369            8 :                 // We actually need to return 'false' here even though this seems like a 'true' case
    2370            8 :                 //   because the normal module resolution algorithm will find this anyway.
    2371            8 :                 return false;
    2372            8 :             }
    2373            8 : 
    2374            8 :             // at least one of declarations should come from non-modified source file
    2375            8 :             const unmodifiedFile = ambientModuleNameToUnmodifiedFileName.get(moduleName.text);
    2376            8 : 
    2377            8 :             if (!unmodifiedFile) {
    2378            8 :                 return false;
    2379            8 :             }
    2380            8 : 
    2381            8 :             if (isTraceEnabled(options, host)) {
    2382            8 :                 trace(host, Diagnostics.Module_0_was_resolved_as_ambient_module_declared_in_1_since_this_file_was_not_modified, moduleName.text, unmodifiedFile);
    2383            8 :             }
    2384            8 :             return true;
    2385            8 :         }
    2386            8 :     }

    2393            8 :             // the best we can do is fallback to the default logic.
