    2461            8 :     function canReuseProjectReferences(): boolean {
    2462            8 :         return !forEachProjectReference(
    2463            8 :             oldProgram!.getProjectReferences(),
    2464            8 :             oldProgram!.getResolvedProjectReferences(),
    2465            8 :             (oldResolvedRef, parent, index) => {
    2466            8 :                 const newRef = (parent ? parent.commandLine.projectReferences : projectReferences)![index];
    2467            8 :                 const newResolvedRef = parseProjectReferenceConfigFile(newRef);
    2468            8 :                 if (oldResolvedRef) {
    2469            8 :                     // Resolved project reference has gone missing or changed
    2470            8 :                     return !newResolvedRef ||
    2471            8 :                         newResolvedRef.sourceFile !== oldResolvedRef.sourceFile ||
    2472            8 :                         !arrayIsEqualTo(oldResolvedRef.commandLine.fileNames, newResolvedRef.commandLine.fileNames);
    2473            8 :                 }
    2474            8 :                 else {
    2475            8 :                     // A previously-unresolved reference may be resolved now
    2476            8 :                     return newResolvedRef !== undefined;
    2477            8 :                 }
    2478            8 :             },
    2479            8 :             (oldProjectReferences, parent) => {
    2480            8 :                 // If array of references is changed, we cant resue old program
    2481            8 :                 const newReferences = parent ? getResolvedProjectReferenceByPath(parent.sourceFile.path)!.commandLine.projectReferences : projectReferences;
    2482            8 :                 return !arrayIsEqualTo(oldProjectReferences, newReferences, projectReferenceIsEqualTo);
    2483            8 :             },
    2484            8 :         );
    2485            8 :     }
    2486            8 : 
    2487            8 :     function tryReuseStructureFromOldProgram(): StructureIsReused {
    2488            8 :         if (!oldProgram) {
    2489            8 :             return StructureIsReused.Not;
    2490            8 :         }
    2491            8 : 
    2492            8 :         // check properties that can affect structure of the program or module resolution strategy
    2493            8 :         // if any of these properties has changed - structure cannot be reused
    2494            8 :         const oldOptions = oldProgram.getCompilerOptions();
    2495            8 :         if (changesAffectModuleResolution(oldOptions, options)) {
    2496            8 :             return StructureIsReused.Not;
    2497            8 :         }
    2498            8 : 
    2499            8 :         // there is an old program, check if we can reuse its structure
    2500            8 :         const oldRootNames = oldProgram.getRootFileNames();
    2501            8 :         if (!arrayIsEqualTo(oldRootNames, rootNames)) {
    2502            8 :             return StructureIsReused.Not;
    2503            8 :         }
    2504            8 : 
    2505            8 :         // Check if any referenced project tsconfig files are different
    2506            8 :         if (!canReuseProjectReferences()) {
    2507            8 :             return StructureIsReused.Not;
    2508            8 :         }
    2509            8 :         if (projectReferences) {
    2510            8 :             resolvedProjectReferences = projectReferences.map(parseProjectReferenceConfigFile);
    2511            8 :         }
    2512            8 : 
    2513            8 :         // check if program source files has changed in the way that can affect structure of the program
    2514            8 :         const newSourceFiles: SourceFile[] = [];
    2515            8 :         const modifiedSourceFiles: SourceFile[] = [];
    2516            8 :         structureIsReused = StructureIsReused.Completely;
    2517            8 : 
    2518            8 :         // If the missing file paths are now present, it can change the progam structure,
    2519            8 :         // and hence cant reuse the structure.
    2520            8 :         // This is same as how we dont reuse the structure if one of the file from old program is now missing
    2521            8 :         if (forEachEntry(oldProgram.getMissingFilePaths(), missingFileName => host.fileExists(missingFileName))) {
    2522            8 :             return StructureIsReused.Not;
    2523            8 :         }
    2524            8 : 
    2525            8 :         const oldSourceFiles = oldProgram.getSourceFiles();
    2526            8 :         const enum SeenPackageName {
    2527            8 :             Exists,
    2528            8 :             Modified,
    2529            8 :         }
    2530            8 :         const seenPackageNames = new Map<string, SeenPackageName>();
    2531            8 : 
    2532            8 :         for (const oldSourceFile of oldSourceFiles) {
    2533            8 :             const sourceFileOptions = getCreateSourceFileOptions(oldSourceFile.fileName, moduleResolutionCache, host, options);
    2534            8 :             let newSourceFile = host.getSourceFileByPath
    2535            8 :                 ? host.getSourceFileByPath(oldSourceFile.fileName, oldSourceFile.resolvedPath, sourceFileOptions, /*onError*/ undefined, shouldCreateNewSourceFile)
    2536            8 :                 : host.getSourceFile(oldSourceFile.fileName, sourceFileOptions, /*onError*/ undefined, shouldCreateNewSourceFile); // TODO: GH#18217
    2537            8 : 
    2538            8 :             if (!newSourceFile) {
    2539            8 :                 return StructureIsReused.Not;
    2540            8 :             }
    2541            8 :             newSourceFile.packageJsonLocations = sourceFileOptions.packageJsonLocations?.length ? sourceFileOptions.packageJsonLocations : undefined;
    2542            8 :             newSourceFile.packageJsonScope = sourceFileOptions.packageJsonScope;
    2543            8 : 
    2544            8 :             Debug.assert(!newSourceFile.redirectInfo, "Host should not return a redirect source file from `getSourceFile`");
    2545            8 : 
    2546            8 :             let fileChanged: boolean;
    2547            8 :             if (oldSourceFile.redirectInfo) {
    2548            8 :                 // We got `newSourceFile` by path, so it is actually for the unredirected file.
    2549            8 :                 // This lets us know if the unredirected file has changed. If it has we should break the redirect.
    2550            8 :                 if (newSourceFile !== oldSourceFile.redirectInfo.unredirected) {
    2551            8 :                     // Underlying file has changed. Might not redirect anymore. Must rebuild program.
    2552            8 :                     return StructureIsReused.Not;
    2553            8 :                 }
    2554            8 :                 fileChanged = false;
    2555            8 :                 newSourceFile = oldSourceFile; // Use the redirect.
    2556            8 :             }
    2557            8 :             else if (oldProgram.redirectTargetsMap.has(oldSourceFile.path)) {
    2558            8 :                 // If a redirected-to source file changes, the redirect may be broken.
    2559            8 :                 if (newSourceFile !== oldSourceFile) {
    2560            8 :                     return StructureIsReused.Not;
    2561            8 :                 }
    2562            8 :                 fileChanged = false;
    2563            8 :             }
    2564            8 :             else {
    2565            8 :                 fileChanged = newSourceFile !== oldSourceFile;
    2566            8 :             }
    2567            8 : 
    2568            8 :             // Since the project references havent changed, its right to set originalFileName and resolvedPath here
    2569            8 :             newSourceFile.path = oldSourceFile.path;
    2570            8 :             newSourceFile.originalFileName = oldSourceFile.originalFileName;
    2571            8 :             newSourceFile.resolvedPath = oldSourceFile.resolvedPath;
    2572            8 :             newSourceFile.fileName = oldSourceFile.fileName;
    2573            8 : 
    2574            8 :             const packageName = oldProgram.sourceFileToPackageName.get(oldSourceFile.path);
    2575            8 :             if (packageName !== undefined) {
    2576            8 :                 // If there are 2 different source files for the same package name and at least one of them changes,
    2577            8 :                 // they might become redirects. So we must rebuild the program.
    2578            8 :                 const prevKind = seenPackageNames.get(packageName);
    2579            8 :                 const newKind = fileChanged ? SeenPackageName.Modified : SeenPackageName.Exists;
    2580            8 :                 if ((prevKind !== undefined && newKind === SeenPackageName.Modified) || prevKind === SeenPackageName.Modified) {
    2581            8 :                     return StructureIsReused.Not;
    2582            8 :                 }
    2583            8 :                 seenPackageNames.set(packageName, newKind);
    2584            8 :             }
    2585            8 : 
    2586            8 :             if (fileChanged) {
    2587            8 :                 if (oldSourceFile.impliedNodeFormat !== newSourceFile.impliedNodeFormat) {
    2588            8 :                     structureIsReused = StructureIsReused.SafeModules;
    2589            8 :                 }
    2590            8 :                 // The `newSourceFile` object was created for the new program.
    2591            8 :                 else if (!arrayIsEqualTo(oldSourceFile.libReferenceDirectives, newSourceFile.libReferenceDirectives, fileReferenceIsEqualTo)) {
    2592            8 :                     // 'lib' references has changed. Matches behavior in changesAffectModuleResolution
    2593            8 :                     structureIsReused = StructureIsReused.SafeModules;
    2594            8 :                 }
    2595            8 :                 else if (oldSourceFile.hasNoDefaultLib !== newSourceFile.hasNoDefaultLib) {
    2596            8 :                     // value of no-default-lib has changed
    2597            8 :                     // this will affect if default library is injected into the list of files
    2598            8 :                     structureIsReused = StructureIsReused.SafeModules;
    2599            8 :                 }
    2600            8 :                 // check tripleslash references
    2601            8 :                 else if (!arrayIsEqualTo(oldSourceFile.referencedFiles, newSourceFile.referencedFiles, fileReferenceIsEqualTo)) {
    2602            8 :                     // tripleslash references has changed
    2603            8 :                     structureIsReused = StructureIsReused.SafeModules;
    2604            8 :                 }
    2605            8 :                 else {
    2606            8 :                     // check imports and module augmentations
    2607            8 :                     collectExternalModuleReferences(newSourceFile);
    2608            8 :                     if (!arrayIsEqualTo(oldSourceFile.imports, newSourceFile.imports, moduleNameIsEqualTo)) {
    2609            8 :                         // imports has changed
    2610            8 :                         structureIsReused = StructureIsReused.SafeModules;
    2611            8 :                     }
    2612            8 :                     else if (!arrayIsEqualTo(oldSourceFile.moduleAugmentations, newSourceFile.moduleAugmentations, moduleNameIsEqualTo)) {
    2613            8 :                         // moduleAugmentations has changed
    2614            8 :                         structureIsReused = StructureIsReused.SafeModules;
    2615            8 :                     }
    2616            8 :                     else if ((oldSourceFile.flags & NodeFlags.PermanentlySetIncrementalFlags) !== (newSourceFile.flags & NodeFlags.PermanentlySetIncrementalFlags)) {
    2617            8 :                         // dynamicImport has changed
    2618            8 :                         structureIsReused = StructureIsReused.SafeModules;
    2619            8 :                     }
    2620            8 :                     else if (!arrayIsEqualTo(oldSourceFile.typeReferenceDirectives, newSourceFile.typeReferenceDirectives, fileReferenceIsEqualTo)) {
    2621            8 :                         // 'types' references has changed
    2622            8 :                         structureIsReused = StructureIsReused.SafeModules;
    2623            8 :                     }
    2624            8 :                 }
    2625            8 : 
    2626            8 :                 // tentatively approve the file
    2627            8 :                 modifiedSourceFiles.push(newSourceFile);
    2628            8 :             }
    2629            8 :             else if (hasInvalidatedResolutions(oldSourceFile.path)) {
    2630            8 :                 // 'module/types' references could have changed
    2631            8 :                 structureIsReused = StructureIsReused.SafeModules;
    2632            8 : 
    2633            8 :                 // add file to the modified list so that we will resolve it later
    2634            8 :                 modifiedSourceFiles.push(newSourceFile);
    2635            8 :             }
    2636            8 :             else {
    2637            8 :                 for (const moduleName of oldSourceFile.ambientModuleNames) {
    2638            8 :                     ambientModuleNameToUnmodifiedFileName.set(moduleName, oldSourceFile.fileName);
    2639            8 :                 }
    2640            8 :             }
    2641            8 : 
    2642            8 :             // if file has passed all checks it should be safe to reuse it
    2643            8 :             newSourceFiles.push(newSourceFile);
    2644            8 :         }
    2645            8 : 
    2646            8 :         if (structureIsReused !== StructureIsReused.Completely) {
    2647            8 :             return structureIsReused;
    2648            8 :         }
    2649            8 : 
    2650            8 :         // try to verify results of module resolution
    2651            8 :         for (const newSourceFile of modifiedSourceFiles) {
    2652            8 :             const moduleNames = getModuleNames(newSourceFile);
    2653            8 :             const resolutions = resolveModuleNamesReusingOldState(moduleNames, newSourceFile);
    2654            8 :             (resolvedModulesProcessing ??= new Map()).set(newSourceFile.path, resolutions);
    2655            8 :             // ensure that module resolution results are still correct
    2656            8 :             const resolutionsChanged = hasChangesInResolutions(
    2657            8 :                 moduleNames,
    2658            8 :                 resolutions,
    2659            8 :                 name => oldProgram.getResolvedModule(newSourceFile, name.text, getModeForUsageLocation(newSourceFile, name)),
    2660            8 :                 moduleResolutionIsEqualTo,
    2661            8 :             );
    2662            8 :             if (resolutionsChanged) structureIsReused = StructureIsReused.SafeModules;
    2663            8 :             const typesReferenceDirectives = newSourceFile.typeReferenceDirectives;
    2664            8 :             const typeReferenceResolutions = resolveTypeReferenceDirectiveNamesReusingOldState(typesReferenceDirectives, newSourceFile);
    2665            8 :             (resolvedTypeReferenceDirectiveNamesProcessing ??= new Map()).set(newSourceFile.path, typeReferenceResolutions);
    2666            8 :             // ensure that types resolutions are still correct
    2667            8 :             const typeReferenceResolutionsChanged = hasChangesInResolutions(
    2668            8 :                 typesReferenceDirectives,
    2669            8 :                 typeReferenceResolutions,
    2670            8 :                 name => oldProgram.getResolvedTypeReferenceDirective(newSourceFile, getTypeReferenceResolutionName(name), getModeForFileReference(name, newSourceFile.impliedNodeFormat)),
    2671            8 :                 typeDirectiveIsEqualTo,
    2672            8 :             );
    2673            8 :             if (typeReferenceResolutionsChanged) structureIsReused = StructureIsReused.SafeModules;
    2674            8 :         }
    2675            8 : 
    2676            8 :         if (structureIsReused !== StructureIsReused.Completely) {
    2677            8 :             return structureIsReused;
    2678            8 :         }
    2679            8 : 
    2680            8 :         if (changesAffectingProgramStructure(oldOptions, options)) {
    2681            8 :             return StructureIsReused.SafeModules;
    2682            8 :         }
    2683            8 : 
    2684            8 :         if (
    2685            8 :             oldProgram.resolvedLibReferences &&
    2686            8 :             forEachEntry(oldProgram.resolvedLibReferences, (resolution, libFileName) => pathForLibFileWorker(libFileName).actual !== resolution.actual)
    2687            8 :         ) {
    2688            8 :             return StructureIsReused.SafeModules;
    2689            8 :         }
    2690            8 : 
    2691            8 :         if (host.hasChangedAutomaticTypeDirectiveNames) {
    2692            8 :             if (host.hasChangedAutomaticTypeDirectiveNames()) return StructureIsReused.SafeModules;
    2693            8 :         }
    2694            8 :         else {
    2695            8 :             automaticTypeDirectiveNames = getAutomaticTypeDirectiveNames(options, host);
    2696            8 :             if (!arrayIsEqualTo(oldProgram.getAutomaticTypeDirectiveNames(), automaticTypeDirectiveNames)) return StructureIsReused.SafeModules;
    2697            8 :         }
    2698            8 :         missingFileNames = oldProgram.getMissingFilePaths();
    2699            8 : 
    2700            8 :         // update fileName -> file mapping
    2701            8 :         Debug.assert(newSourceFiles.length === oldProgram.getSourceFiles().length);
    2702            8 :         for (const newSourceFile of newSourceFiles) {
    2703            8 :             filesByName.set(newSourceFile.path, newSourceFile);
    2704            8 :         }
    2705            8 :         const oldFilesByNameMap = oldProgram.getFilesByNameMap();
    2706            8 :         oldFilesByNameMap.forEach((oldFile, path) => {
    2707            8 :             if (!oldFile) {
    2708            8 :                 filesByName.set(path, oldFile);
    2709            8 :                 return;
    2710            8 :             }
    2711            8 :             if (oldFile.path === path) {
    2712            8 :                 // Set the file as found during node modules search if it was found that way in old progra,
    2713            8 :                 if (oldProgram.isSourceFileFromExternalLibrary(oldFile)) {
    2714            8 :                     sourceFilesFoundSearchingNodeModules.set(oldFile.path, true);
    2715            8 :                 }
    2716            8 :                 return;
    2717            8 :             }
    2718            8 :             filesByName.set(path, filesByName.get(oldFile.path));
    2719            8 :         });
    2720            8 : 
    2721            8 :         files = newSourceFiles;
    2722            8 :         fileReasons = oldProgram.getFileIncludeReasons();
    2723            8 :         fileProcessingDiagnostics = oldProgram.getFileProcessingDiagnostics();
    2724            8 :         automaticTypeDirectiveNames = oldProgram.getAutomaticTypeDirectiveNames();
    2725            8 :         automaticTypeDirectiveResolutions = oldProgram.getAutomaticTypeDirectiveResolutions();
    2726            8 : 
    2727            8 :         sourceFileToPackageName = oldProgram.sourceFileToPackageName;
    2728            8 :         redirectTargetsMap = oldProgram.redirectTargetsMap;
    2729            8 :         usesUriStyleNodeCoreModules = oldProgram.usesUriStyleNodeCoreModules;
    2730            8 :         resolvedModules = oldProgram.resolvedModules;
    2731            8 :         resolvedTypeReferenceDirectiveNames = oldProgram.resolvedTypeReferenceDirectiveNames;
    2732            8 :         resolvedLibReferences = oldProgram.resolvedLibReferences;
    2733            8 :         packageMap = oldProgram.getCurrentPackagesMap();
    2734            8 : 
    2735            8 :         return StructureIsReused.Completely;
    2736            8 :     }
    2737            8 : 
    2738            8 :     function getEmitHost(writeFileCallback?: WriteFileCallback): EmitHost {
    2739            8 :         return {
    2740            8 :             getCanonicalFileName,
    2741            8 :             getCommonSourceDirectory: program.getCommonSourceDirectory,
    2742            8 :             getCompilerOptions: program.getCompilerOptions,
    2743            8 :             getCurrentDirectory: () => currentDirectory,
    2744            8 :             getSourceFile: program.getSourceFile,
    2745            8 :             getSourceFileByPath: program.getSourceFileByPath,
    2746            8 :             getSourceFiles: program.getSourceFiles,
    2747            8 :             isSourceFileFromExternalLibrary,
    2748            8 :             getResolvedProjectReferenceToRedirect,
    2749            8 :             getProjectReferenceRedirect,
    2750            8 :             isSourceOfProjectReferenceRedirect,
    2751            8 :             getSymlinkCache,
    2752            8 :             writeFile: writeFileCallback || writeFile,
    2753            8 :             isEmitBlocked,
    2754            8 :             shouldTransformImportCall,
    2755            8 :             getEmitModuleFormatOfFile,
    2756            8 :             getDefaultResolutionModeForFile,
    2757            8 :             getModeForResolutionAtIndex,
    2758            8 :             readFile: f => host.readFile(f),
    2759            8 :             fileExists: f => {
    2760            8 :                 // Use local caches
    2761            8 :                 const path = toPath(f);
    2762            8 :                 if (getSourceFileByPath(path)) return true;
    2763            8 :                 if (missingFileNames.has(path)) return false;
    2764            8 :                 // Before falling back to the host
    2765            8 :                 return host.fileExists(f);
    2766            8 :             },
    2767            8 :             realpath: maybeBind(host, host.realpath),
    2768            8 :             useCaseSensitiveFileNames: () => host.useCaseSensitiveFileNames(),
    2769            8 :             getBuildInfo: () => program.getBuildInfo?.(),
    2770            8 :             getSourceFileFromReference: (file, ref) => program.getSourceFileFromReference(file, ref),
    2771            8 :             redirectTargetsMap,
    2772            8 :             getFileIncludeReasons: program.getFileIncludeReasons,
    2773            8 :             createHash: maybeBind(host, host.createHash),
    2774            8 :             getModuleResolutionCache: () => program.getModuleResolutionCache(),
    2775            8 :             trace: maybeBind(host, host.trace),
    2776            8 :         };
    2777            8 :     }

    2790            8 :     function emitBuildInfo(writeFileCallback?: WriteFileCallback): EmitResult {
    2791            8 :         tracing?.push(tracing.Phase.Emit, "emitBuildInfo", {}, /*separateBeginAndEnd*/ true);
    2792            8 :         performance.mark("beforeEmit");
    2793            8 :         const emitResult = emitFiles(
    2794            8 :             notImplementedResolver,
    2795            8 :             getEmitHost(writeFileCallback),
    2796            8 :             /*targetSourceFile*/ undefined,
    2797            8 :             /*transformers*/ noTransformers,
    2798            8 :             /*emitOnly*/ false,
    2799            8 :             /*onlyBuildInfo*/ true,
    2800            8 :         );
    2801            8 : 
    2802            8 :         performance.mark("afterEmit");
    2803            8 :         performance.measure("Emit", "beforeEmit", "afterEmit");
    2804            8 :         tracing?.pop();
    2805            8 :         return emitResult;
    2806            8 :     }

    2816            8 :     function isSourceFileFromExternalLibrary(file: SourceFile): boolean {
    2817            8 :         return !!sourceFilesFoundSearchingNodeModules.get(file.path);
    2818            8 :     }
    2819            8 : 
    2820            8 :     function isSourceFileDefaultLibrary(file: SourceFile): boolean {
    2821            8 :         if (!file.isDeclarationFile) {
    2822            8 :             return false;
    2823            8 :         }
    2824            8 : 
    2825            8 :         if (file.hasNoDefaultLib) {
    2826            8 :             return true;
    2827            8 :         }
    2828            8 : 
    2829            8 :         if (!options.noLib) {
    2830            8 :             return false;
    2831            8 :         }
    2832            8 : 
    2833            8 :         // If '--lib' is not specified, include default library file according to '--target'
    2834            8 :         // otherwise, using options specified in '--lib' instead of '--target' default library file
    2835            8 :         const equalityComparer = host.useCaseSensitiveFileNames() ? equateStringsCaseSensitive : equateStringsCaseInsensitive;
    2836            8 :         if (!options.lib) {
    2837            8 :             return equalityComparer(file.fileName, getDefaultLibraryFileName());
    2838            8 :         }
    2839            8 :         else {
    2840            8 :             return some(options.lib, libFileName => equalityComparer(file.fileName, resolvedLibReferences!.get(libFileName)!.actual));
    2841            8 :         }
    2842            8 :     }

    2844            8 :     function getTypeChecker() {
    2845            8 :         return typeChecker || (typeChecker = createTypeChecker(program));
    2846            8 :     }

    2848            8 :     function emit(
    2849            8 :         sourceFile?: SourceFile,
    2850            8 :         writeFileCallback?: WriteFileCallback,
    2851            8 :         cancellationToken?: CancellationToken,
    2852            8 :         emitOnly?: boolean | EmitOnly,
    2853            8 :         transformers?: CustomTransformers,
    2854            8 :         forceDtsEmit?: boolean,
    2855            8 :         skipBuildInfo?: boolean,
    2856            8 :     ): EmitResult {
    2857            8 :         tracing?.push(tracing.Phase.Emit, "emit", { path: sourceFile?.path }, /*separateBeginAndEnd*/ true);
    2858            8 :         const result = runWithCancellationToken(() =>
    2859            8 :             emitWorker(
    2860            8 :                 program,
    2861            8 :                 sourceFile,
    2862            8 :                 writeFileCallback,
    2863            8 :                 cancellationToken,
    2864            8 :                 emitOnly,
    2865            8 :                 transformers,
    2866            8 :                 forceDtsEmit,
    2867            8 :                 skipBuildInfo,
    2868            8 :             )
    2869            8 :         );
    2870            8 :         tracing?.pop();
    2871            8 :         return result;
    2872            8 :     }
    2873            8 : 
    2874            8 :     function isEmitBlocked(emitFileName: string): boolean {
    2875            8 :         return hasEmitBlockingDiagnostics.has(toPath(emitFileName));
    2876            8 :     }
    2877            8 : 
    2878            8 :     function emitWorker(
    2879            8 :         program: Program,
    2880            8 :         sourceFile: SourceFile | undefined,
    2881            8 :         writeFileCallback: WriteFileCallback | undefined,
    2882            8 :         cancellationToken: CancellationToken | undefined,
    2883            8 :         emitOnly: boolean | EmitOnly | undefined,
    2884            8 :         customTransformers: CustomTransformers | undefined,
    2885            8 :         forceDtsEmit: boolean | undefined,
    2886            8 :         skipBuildInfo: boolean | undefined,
    2887            8 :     ): EmitResult {
    2888            8 :         if (!forceDtsEmit) {
    2889            8 :             const result = handleNoEmitOptions(program, sourceFile, writeFileCallback, cancellationToken);
    2890            8 :             if (result) return result;
    2891            8 :         }
    2892            8 : 
    2893            8 :         // Create the emit resolver outside of the "emitTime" tracking code below.  That way
    2894            8 :         // any cost associated with it (like type checking) are appropriate associated with
    2895            8 :         // the type-checking counter.
    2896            8 :         //
    2897            8 :         // If the -out option is specified, we should not pass the source file to getEmitResolver.
    2898            8 :         // This is because in the -out scenario all files need to be emitted, and therefore all
    2899            8 :         // files need to be type checked. And the way to specify that all files need to be type
    2900            8 :         // checked is to not pass the file to getEmitResolver.
    2901            8 :         const typeChecker = getTypeChecker();
    2902            8 :         const emitResolver = typeChecker.getEmitResolver(
    2903            8 :             options.outFile ? undefined : sourceFile,
    2904            8 :             cancellationToken,
    2905            8 :             emitResolverSkipsTypeChecking(emitOnly, forceDtsEmit),
    2906            8 :         );
    2907            8 : 
    2908            8 :         performance.mark("beforeEmit");
    2909            8 : 
    2910            8 :         const emitResult = typeChecker.runWithCancellationToken(
    2911            8 :             cancellationToken,
    2912            8 :             () =>
    2913            8 :                 emitFiles(
    2914            8 :                     emitResolver,
    2915            8 :                     getEmitHost(writeFileCallback),
    2916            8 :                     sourceFile,
    2917            8 :                     getTransformers(options, customTransformers, emitOnly),
    2918            8 :                     emitOnly,
    2919            8 :                     /*onlyBuildInfo*/ false,
    2920            8 :                     forceDtsEmit,
    2921            8 :                     skipBuildInfo,
    2922            8 :                 ),
    2923            8 :         );
    2924            8 : 
    2925            8 :         performance.mark("afterEmit");
    2926            8 :         performance.measure("Emit", "beforeEmit", "afterEmit");
    2927            8 :         return emitResult;
    2928            8 :     }
    2929            8 : 
    2930            8 :     function getSourceFile(fileName: string): SourceFile | undefined {

    2932            8 :     }

    2938            8 :     function getDiagnosticsHelper<T extends Diagnostic>(
    2939            8 :         sourceFile: SourceFile | undefined,
    2940            8 :         getDiagnostics: (sourceFile: SourceFile, cancellationToken: CancellationToken | undefined) => readonly T[],
    2941            8 :         cancellationToken: CancellationToken | undefined,
    2942            8 :     ): readonly T[] {
    2943            8 :         if (sourceFile) {
    2944            8 :             return sortAndDeduplicateDiagnostics(getDiagnostics(sourceFile, cancellationToken));
    2945            8 :         }
    2946            8 :         return sortAndDeduplicateDiagnostics(flatMap(program.getSourceFiles(), sourceFile => {
    2947            8 :             if (cancellationToken) {
    2948            8 :                 cancellationToken.throwIfCancellationRequested();
    2949            8 :             }
    2950            8 :             return getDiagnostics(sourceFile, cancellationToken);
    2951            8 :         }));
    2952            8 :     }

    2962            8 :     function getCachedSemanticDiagnostics(sourceFile?: SourceFile): readonly Diagnostic[] | undefined {

    2965            8 :             : cachedBindAndCheckDiagnosticsForFile.allDiagnostics;

    2972            8 :     function getProgramDiagnostics(sourceFile: SourceFile): readonly Diagnostic[] {
    2973            8 :         if (skipTypeChecking(sourceFile, options, program)) {
    2974            8 :             return emptyArray;
    2975            8 :         }
    2976            8 : 
    2977            8 :         const programDiagnosticsInFile = updateAndGetProgramDiagnostics().getDiagnostics(sourceFile.fileName);
    2978            8 :         if (!sourceFile.commentDirectives?.length) {
    2979            8 :             return programDiagnosticsInFile;
    2980            8 :         }
    2981            8 : 
    2982            8 :         return getDiagnosticsWithPrecedingDirectives(sourceFile, sourceFile.commentDirectives, programDiagnosticsInFile).diagnostics;
    2983            8 :     }
    2984            8 : 
    2985            8 :     function getDeclarationDiagnostics(sourceFile?: SourceFile, cancellationToken?: CancellationToken): readonly DiagnosticWithLocation[] {
    2986            8 :         const options = program.getCompilerOptions();
    2987            8 :         // collect diagnostics from the program only once if either no source file was specified or out/outFile is set (bundled emit)
    2988            8 :         if (!sourceFile || options.outFile) {
    2989            8 :             return getDeclarationDiagnosticsWorker(sourceFile, cancellationToken);
    2990            8 :         }
    2991            8 :         else {
    2992            8 :             return getDiagnosticsHelper(sourceFile, getDeclarationDiagnosticsForFile, cancellationToken);
    2993            8 :         }
    2994            8 :     }

    2996            8 :     function getSyntacticDiagnosticsForFile(sourceFile: SourceFile): readonly DiagnosticWithLocation[] {
    2997            8 :         // For JavaScript files, we report semantic errors for using TypeScript-only
    2998            8 :         // constructs from within a JavaScript file as syntactic errors.
    2999            8 :         if (isSourceFileJS(sourceFile)) {
    3000            8 :             if (!sourceFile.additionalSyntacticDiagnostics) {
    3001            8 :                 sourceFile.additionalSyntacticDiagnostics = getJSSyntacticDiagnosticsForFile(sourceFile);
    3002            8 :             }
    3003            8 :             return concatenate(sourceFile.additionalSyntacticDiagnostics, sourceFile.parseDiagnostics);
    3004            8 :         }
    3005            8 :         return sourceFile.parseDiagnostics;
    3006            8 :     }
    3007            8 : 
    3008            8 :     function runWithCancellationToken<T>(func: () => T): T {
    3009            8 :         try {
    3010            8 :             return func();
    3011            8 :         }
    3012            8 :         catch (e) {
    3013            8 :             if (e instanceof OperationCanceledException) {
    3014            8 :                 // We were canceled while performing the operation.  Because our type checker
    3015            8 :                 // might be a bad state, we need to throw it away.
    3016            8 :                 typeChecker = undefined!;
    3017            8 :             }
    3018            8 : 
    3019            8 :             throw e;
    3020            8 :         }
    3021            8 :     }
    3022            8 : 
    3023            8 :     function getSemanticDiagnosticsForFile(sourceFile: SourceFile, cancellationToken: CancellationToken | undefined): readonly Diagnostic[] {
    3024            8 :         return concatenate(
    3025            8 :             filterSemanticDiagnostics(getBindAndCheckDiagnosticsForFile(sourceFile, cancellationToken), options),
    3026            8 :             getProgramDiagnostics(sourceFile),
    3027            8 :         );
    3028            8 :     }
    3029            8 : 
    3030            8 :     function getBindAndCheckDiagnosticsForFile(sourceFile: SourceFile, cancellationToken: CancellationToken | undefined): readonly Diagnostic[] {
    3031            8 :         return getAndCacheDiagnostics(sourceFile, cancellationToken, cachedBindAndCheckDiagnosticsForFile, getBindAndCheckDiagnosticsForFileNoCache);
    3032            8 :     }
    3033            8 : 
    3034            8 :     function getBindAndCheckDiagnosticsForFileNoCache(sourceFile: SourceFile, cancellationToken: CancellationToken | undefined): readonly Diagnostic[] {
    3035            8 :         return runWithCancellationToken(() => {
    3036            8 :             if (skipTypeChecking(sourceFile, options, program)) {
    3037            8 :                 return emptyArray;
    3038            8 :             }
    3039            8 : 
    3040            8 :             const typeChecker = getTypeChecker();
    3041            8 : 
    3042            8 :             Debug.assert(!!sourceFile.bindDiagnostics);
    3043            8 : 
    3044            8 :             const isJs = sourceFile.scriptKind === ScriptKind.JS || sourceFile.scriptKind === ScriptKind.JSX;
    3045            8 :             const isCheckJs = isJs && isCheckJsEnabledForFile(sourceFile, options);
    3046            8 :             const isPlainJs = isPlainJsFile(sourceFile, options.checkJs);
    3047            8 : 
    3048            8 :             // By default, only type-check .ts, .tsx, Deferred, plain JS, checked JS and External
    3049            8 :             // - plain JS: .js files with no // ts-check and checkJs: undefined
    3050            8 :             // - check JS: .js files with either // ts-check or checkJs: true
    3051            8 :             // - external: files that are added by plugins
    3052            8 :             let bindDiagnostics = sourceFile.bindDiagnostics;
    3053            8 :             let checkDiagnostics = typeChecker.getDiagnostics(sourceFile, cancellationToken);
    3054            8 :             if (isPlainJs) {
    3055            8 :                 bindDiagnostics = filter(bindDiagnostics, d => plainJSErrors.has(d.code));
    3056            8 :                 checkDiagnostics = filter(checkDiagnostics, d => plainJSErrors.has(d.code));
    3057            8 :             }
    3058            8 :             // skip ts-expect-error errors in plain JS files, and skip JSDoc errors except in checked JS
    3059            8 :             return getMergedBindAndCheckDiagnostics(sourceFile, !isPlainJs, bindDiagnostics, checkDiagnostics, isCheckJs ? sourceFile.jsDocDiagnostics : undefined);
    3060            8 :         });

    3063            8 :     function getMergedBindAndCheckDiagnostics(sourceFile: SourceFile, includeBindAndCheckDiagnostics: boolean, ...allDiagnostics: (readonly Diagnostic[] | undefined)[]) {

    3078            8 :     /**
    3079            8 :      * Creates a map of comment directives along with the diagnostics immediately preceded by one of them.
    3080            8 :      * Comments that match to any of those diagnostics are marked as used.
    3081            8 :      */
    3082            8 :     function getDiagnosticsWithPrecedingDirectives(sourceFile: SourceFile, commentDirectives: CommentDirective[], flatDiagnostics: Diagnostic[]) {
    3083            8 :         // Diagnostics are only reported if there is no comment directive preceding them
    3084            8 :         // This will modify the directives map by marking "used" ones with a corresponding diagnostic
    3085            8 :         const directives = createCommentDirectivesMap(sourceFile, commentDirectives);
    3086            8 :         const diagnostics = flatDiagnostics.filter(diagnostic => markPrecedingCommentDirectiveLine(diagnostic, directives) === -1);
    3087            8 :

    3097            8 :     /**
    3098            8 :      * @returns The line index marked as preceding the diagnostic, or -1 if none was.
    3099            8 :      */
    3100            8 :     function markPrecedingCommentDirectiveLine(diagnostic: Diagnostic, directives: CommentDirectivesMap) {
    3101            8 :         const { file, start } = diagnostic;
    3102            8 :         if (!file) {
    3103            8 :             return -1;
    3104            8 :         }
    3105            8 : 
    3106            8 :         // Start out with the line just before the text
    3107            8 :         const lineStarts = getLineStarts(file);
    3108            8 :         let line = computeLineAndCharacterOfPosition(lineStarts, start!).line - 1; // TODO: GH#18217
    3109            8 :         while (line >= 0) {
    3110            8 :             // As soon as that line is known to have a comment directive, use that
    3111            8 :             if (directives.markUsed(line)) {
    3112            8 :                 return line;
    3113            8 :             }
    3114            8 : 
    3115            8 :             // Stop searching if the line is not empty and not a comment
    3116            8 :             const lineText = file.text.slice(lineStarts[line], lineStarts[line + 1]).trim();
    3117            8 :             if (lineText !== "" && !/^(\s*)\/\/(.*)$/.test(lineText)) {
    3118            8 :                 return -1;
    3119            8 :             }
    3120            8 : 
    3121            8 :             line--;
    3122            8 :         }
    3123            8 : 
    3124            8 :         return -1;
    3125            8 :     }

    3135            8 :             function walk(node: Node, parent: Node) {

    3137            8 :                 // Otherwise break to visit each child

    3238            8 :             function walkArray(nodes: NodeArray<Node>, parent: Node) {
    3239            8 :                 if (canHaveIllegalDecorators(parent)) {
    3240            8 :                     const decorator = find(parent.modifiers, isDecorator);
    3241            8 :                     if (decorator) {
    3242            8 :                         // report illegal decorator
    3243            8 :                         diagnostics.push(createDiagnosticForNode(decorator, Diagnostics.Decorators_are_not_valid_here));
    3244            8 :                     }
    3245            8 :                 }
    3246            8 :                 else if (canHaveDecorators(parent) && parent.modifiers) {
    3247            8 :                     const decoratorIndex = findIndex(parent.modifiers, isDecorator);
    3248            8 :                     if (decoratorIndex >= 0) {
    3249            8 :                         if (isParameter(parent) && !options.experimentalDecorators) {
    3250            8 :                             // report illegall decorator on parameter
    3251            8 :                             diagnostics.push(createDiagnosticForNode(parent.modifiers[decoratorIndex], Diagnostics.Decorators_are_not_valid_here));
    3252            8 :                         }
    3253            8 :                         else if (isClassDeclaration(parent)) {
    3254            8 :                             const exportIndex = findIndex(parent.modifiers, isExportModifier);
    3255            8 :                             if (exportIndex >= 0) {
    3256            8 :                                 const defaultIndex = findIndex(parent.modifiers, isDefaultModifier);
    3257            8 :                                 if (decoratorIndex > exportIndex && defaultIndex >= 0 && decoratorIndex < defaultIndex) {
    3258            8 :                                     // report illegal decorator between `export` and `default`
    3259            8 :                                     diagnostics.push(createDiagnosticForNode(parent.modifiers[decoratorIndex], Diagnostics.Decorators_are_not_valid_here));
    3260            8 :                                 }
    3261            8 :                                 else if (exportIndex >= 0 && decoratorIndex < exportIndex) {
    3262            8 :                                     const trailingDecoratorIndex = findIndex(parent.modifiers, isDecorator, exportIndex);
    3263            8 :                                     if (trailingDecoratorIndex >= 0) {

    3391            8 :     function getAndCacheDiagnostics<T extends SourceFile | undefined, U extends Diagnostic>(
    3392            8 :         sourceFile: T,
    3393            8 :         cancellationToken: CancellationToken | undefined,
    3394            8 :         cache: DiagnosticCache<U>,
    3395            8 :         getDiagnostics: (sourceFile: T, cancellationToken: CancellationToken | undefined) => readonly U[],
    3396            8 :     ): readonly U[] {
    3397            8 :         const cachedResult = sourceFile
    3398            8 :             ? cache.perFile?.get(sourceFile.path)
    3399            8 :             : cache.allDiagnostics;
    3400            8 : 
    3401            8 :         if (cachedResult) {
    3402            8 :             return cachedResult;
    3403            8 :         }
    3404            8 :         const result = getDiagnostics(sourceFile, cancellationToken);
    3405            8 :         if (sourceFile) {
    3406            8 :             (cache.perFile || (cache.perFile = new Map())).set(sourceFile.path, result);
    3407            8 :         }
    3408            8 :         else {
    3409            8 :             cache.allDiagnostics = result;
    3410            8 :         }
    3411            8 :         return result;
    3412            8 :     }

    3456            8 :     function createSyntheticImport(text: string, file: SourceFile) {
    3457            8 :         const externalHelpersModuleReference = factory.createStringLiteral(text);
    3458            8 :         const importDecl = factory.createImportDeclaration(/*modifiers*/ undefined, /*importClause*/ undefined, externalHelpersModuleReference);
    3459            8 :         addInternalEmitFlags(importDecl, InternalEmitFlags.NeverApplyImportHelper);
    3460            8 :         setParent(externalHelpersModuleReference, importDecl);
    3461            8 :         setParent(importDecl, file);
    3462            8 :         // explicitly unset the synthesized flag on these declarations so the checker API will answer questions about them
    3463            8 :         // (which is required to build the dependency graph for incremental emit)
    3464            8 :         (externalHelpersModuleReference as Mutable<Node>).flags &= ~NodeFlags.Synthesized;
    3465            8 :         (importDecl as Mutable<Node>).flags &= ~NodeFlags.Synthesized;
    3466            8 :         return externalHelpersModuleReference;
    3467            8 :     }
    3468            8 : 
    3469            8 :     function collectExternalModuleReferences(file: SourceFile): void {
    3470            8 :         if (file.imports) {
    3471            8 :             return;
    3472            8 :         }
    3473            8 : 
    3474            8 :         const isJavaScriptFile = isSourceFileJS(file);
    3475            8 :         const isExternalModuleFile = isExternalModule(file);
    3476            8 : 
    3477            8 :         // file.imports may not be undefined if there exists dynamic import
    3478            8 :         let imports: StringLiteralLike[] | undefined;
    3479            8 :         let moduleAugmentations: (StringLiteral | Identifier)[] | undefined;
    3480            8 :         let ambientModules: string[] | undefined;
    3481            8 : 
    3482            8 :         // If we are importing helpers, we need to add a synthetic reference to resolve the
    3483            8 :         // helpers library. (A JavaScript file without `externalModuleIndicator` set might be
    3484            8 :         // a CommonJS module; `commonJsModuleIndicator` doesn't get set until the binder has
    3485            8 :         // run. We synthesize a helpers import for it just in case; it will never be used if
    3486            8 :         // the binder doesn't find and set a `commonJsModuleIndicator`.)
    3487            8 :         if (isJavaScriptFile || (!file.isDeclarationFile && (getIsolatedModules(options) || isExternalModule(file)))) {
    3488            8 :             if (options.importHelpers) {
    3489            8 :                 // synthesize 'import "tslib"' declaration
    3490            8 :                 imports = [createSyntheticImport(externalHelpersModuleNameText, file)];
    3491            8 :             }
    3492            8 :             const jsxImport = getJSXRuntimeImport(getJSXImplicitImportBase(options, file), options);
    3493            8 :             if (jsxImport) {
    3494            8 :                 // synthesize `import "base/jsx-runtime"` declaration
    3495            8 :                 (imports ||= []).push(createSyntheticImport(jsxImport, file));
    3496            8 :             }
    3497            8 :         }
    3498            8 : 
    3499            8 :         for (const node of file.statements) {
    3500            8 :             collectModuleReferences(node, /*inAmbientModule*/ false);
    3501            8 :         }
    3502            8 : 
    3503            8 :         if ((file.flags & NodeFlags.PossiblyContainsDynamicImport) || isJavaScriptFile) {
    3504            8 :             collectDynamicImportOrRequireOrJsDocImportCalls(file);
    3505            8 :         }
    3506            8 : 
    3507            8 :         file.imports = imports || emptyArray;
    3508            8 :         file.moduleAugmentations = moduleAugmentations || emptyArray;
    3509            8 :         file.ambientModuleNames = ambientModules || emptyArray;
    3510            8 : 
    3511            8 :         return;
    3512            8 : 
    3513            8 :         function collectModuleReferences(node: Statement, inAmbientModule: boolean): void {
    3514            8 :             if (isAnyImportOrReExport(node)) {
    3515            8 :                 const moduleNameExpr = getExternalModuleName(node);
    3516            8 :                 // TypeScript 1.0 spec (April 2014): 12.1.6
    3517            8 :                 // An ExternalImportDeclaration in an AmbientExternalModuleDeclaration may reference other external modules
    3518            8 :                 // only through top - level external module names. Relative external module names are not permitted.
    3519            8 :                 if (moduleNameExpr && isStringLiteral(moduleNameExpr) && moduleNameExpr.text && (!inAmbientModule || !isExternalModuleNameRelative(moduleNameExpr.text))) {
    3520            8 :                     setParentRecursive(node, /*incremental*/ false); // we need parent data on imports before the program is fully bound, so we ensure it's set here
    3521            8 :                     imports = append(imports, moduleNameExpr);
    3522            8 :                     if (!usesUriStyleNodeCoreModules && currentNodeModulesDepth === 0 && !file.isDeclarationFile) {
    3523            8 :                         usesUriStyleNodeCoreModules = startsWith(moduleNameExpr.text, "node:");
    3524            8 :                     }
    3525            8 :                 }
    3526            8 :             }
    3527            8 :             else if (isModuleDeclaration(node)) {
    3528            8 :                 if (isAmbientModule(node) && (inAmbientModule || hasSyntacticModifier(node, ModifierFlags.Ambient) || file.isDeclarationFile)) {
    3529            8 :                     (node.name as Mutable<Node>).parent = node;
    3530            8 :                     const nameText = getTextOfIdentifierOrLiteral(node.name);
    3531            8 :                     // Ambient module declarations can be interpreted as augmentations for some existing external modules.
    3532            8 :                     // This will happen in two cases:
    3533            8 :                     // - if current file is external module then module augmentation is a ambient module declaration defined in the top level scope
    3534            8 :                     // - if current file is not external module then module augmentation is an ambient module declaration with non-relative module name
    3535            8 :                     //   immediately nested in top level ambient module declaration .
    3536            8 :                     if (isExternalModuleFile || (inAmbientModule && !isExternalModuleNameRelative(nameText))) {
    3537            8 :                         (moduleAugmentations || (moduleAugmentations = [])).push(node.name);
    3538            8 :                     }
    3539            8 :                     else if (!inAmbientModule) {
    3540            8 :                         if (file.isDeclarationFile) {
    3541            8 :                             // for global .d.ts files record name of ambient module
    3542            8 :                             (ambientModules || (ambientModules = [])).push(nameText);
    3543            8 :                         }
    3544            8 :                         // An AmbientExternalModuleDeclaration declares an external module.
    3545            8 :                         // This type of declaration is permitted only in the global module.
    3546            8 :                         // The StringLiteral must specify a top - level external module name.
    3547            8 :                         // Relative external module names are not permitted
    3548            8 : 
    3549            8 :                         // NOTE: body of ambient module is always a module block, if it exists
    3550            8 :                         const body = (node as ModuleDeclaration).body as ModuleBlock;
    3551            8 :                         if (body) {
    3552            8 :                             for (const statement of body.statements) {
    3553            8 :                                 collectModuleReferences(statement, /*inAmbientModule*/ true);
    3554            8 :                             }
    3555            8 :                         }
    3556            8 :                     }
    3557            8 :                 }
    3558            8 :             }
    3559            8 :         }
    3560            8 : 
    3561            8 :         function collectDynamicImportOrRequireOrJsDocImportCalls(file: SourceFile) {
    3562            8 :             const r = /import|require/g;
    3563            8 :             while (r.exec(file.text) !== null) { // eslint-disable-line no-restricted-syntax
    3564            8 :                 const node = getNodeAtPosition(file, r.lastIndex);
    3565            8 :                 if (isJavaScriptFile && isRequireCall(node, /*requireStringLiteralLikeArgument*/ true)) {
    3566            8 :                     setParentRecursive(node, /*incremental*/ false); // we need parent data on imports before the program is fully bound, so we ensure it's set here
    3567            8 :                     imports = append(imports, node.arguments[0]);
    3568            8 :                 }
    3569            8 :                 // we have to check the argument list has length of at least 1. We will still have to process these even though we have parsing error.
    3570            8 :                 else if (isImportCall(node) && node.arguments.length >= 1 && isStringLiteralLike(node.arguments[0])) {
    3571            8 :                     setParentRecursive(node, /*incremental*/ false); // we need parent data on imports before the program is fully bound, so we ensure it's set here
    3572            8 :                     imports = append(imports, node.arguments[0]);
    3573            8 :                 }
    3574            8 :                 else if (isLiteralImportTypeNode(node)) {
    3575            8 :                     setParentRecursive(node, /*incremental*/ false); // we need parent data on imports before the program is fully bound, so we ensure it's set here
    3576            8 :                     imports = append(imports, node.argument.literal);
    3577            8 :                 }
    3578            8 :                 else if (isJavaScriptFile && isJSDocImportTag(node)) {
    3579            8 :                     const moduleNameExpr = getExternalModuleName(node);
    3580            8 :                     if (moduleNameExpr && isStringLiteral(moduleNameExpr) && moduleNameExpr.text) {
    3581            8 :                         setParentRecursive(node, /*incremental*/ false);
    3582            8 :                         imports = append(imports, moduleNameExpr);
    3583            8 :                     }
    3584            8 :                 }
    3585            8 :             }
    3586            8 :         }
    3587            8 : 
    3588            8 :         /** Returns a token if position is in [start-of-leading-trivia, end), includes JSDoc only in JS files */
    3589            8 :         function getNodeAtPosition(sourceFile: SourceFile, position: number): Node {
    3590            8 :             let current: Node = sourceFile;
    3591            8 :             const getContainingChild = (child: Node) => {
    3592            8 :                 if (child.pos <= position && (position < child.end || (position === child.end && (child.kind === SyntaxKind.EndOfFileToken)))) {
    3593            8 :                     return child;
    3594            8 :                 }
    3595            8 :             };
    3596            8 :             while (true) {
    3597            8 :                 const child = isJavaScriptFile && hasJSDocNodes(current) && forEach(current.jsDoc, getContainingChild) || forEachChild(current, getContainingChild);
    3598            8 :                 if (!child) {
    3599            8 :                     return current;
    3600            8 :                 }
    3601            8 :                 current = child;
    3602            8 :             }
    3603            8 :         }
    3604            8 :     }
    3605            8 : 
    3606            8 :     function getLibFileFromReference(ref: FileReference) {
    3607            8 :         const libFileName = getLibFileNameFromLibReference(ref);
    3608            8 :         const actualFileName = libFileName && resolvedLibReferences?.get(libFileName)?.actual;
    3609            8 :         return actualFileName !== undefined ? getSourceFile(actualFileName) : undefined;
    3610            8 :     }

    3612            8 :     /** This should have similar behavior to 'processSourceFile' without diagnostics or mutation. */
    3613            8 :     function getSourceFileFromReference(referencingFile: SourceFile, ref: FileReference): SourceFile | undefined {
    3614            8 :         return getSourceFileFromReferenceWorker(resolveTripleslashReference(ref.fileName, referencingFile.fileName), getSourceFile);
    3615            8 :     }
    3616            8 : 
    3617            8 :     function getSourceFileFromReferenceWorker(
    3618            8 :         fileName: string,
    3619            8 :         getSourceFile: (fileName: string) => SourceFile | undefined,
    3620            8 :         fail?: (diagnostic: DiagnosticMessage, ...argument: string[]) => void,
    3621            8 :         reason?: FileIncludeReason,
    3622            8 :     ): SourceFile | undefined {
    3623            8 :         if (hasExtension(fileName)) {
    3624            8 :             const canonicalFileName = host.getCanonicalFileName(fileName);
    3625            8 :             if (!options.allowNonTsExtensions && !forEach(flatten(supportedExtensionsWithJsonIfResolveJsonModule), extension => fileExtensionIs(canonicalFileName, extension))) {
    3626            8 :                 if (fail) {
    3627            8 :                     if (hasJSFileExtension(canonicalFileName)) {
    3628            8 :                         fail(Diagnostics.File_0_is_a_JavaScript_file_Did_you_mean_to_enable_the_allowJs_option, fileName);
    3629            8 :                     }
    3630            8 :                     else {
    3631            8 :                         fail(Diagnostics.File_0_has_an_unsupported_extension_The_only_supported_extensions_are_1, fileName, "'" + flatten(supportedExtensions).join("', '") + "'");
    3632            8 :                     }
    3633            8 :                 }
    3634            8 :                 return undefined;
    3635            8 :             }
    3636            8 : 
    3637            8 :             const sourceFile = getSourceFile(fileName);
    3638            8 :             if (fail) {
    3639            8 :                 if (!sourceFile) {
    3640            8 :                     const redirect = getProjectReferenceRedirect(fileName);
    3641            8 :                     if (redirect) {
    3642            8 :                         fail(Diagnostics.Output_file_0_has_not_been_built_from_source_file_1, redirect, fileName);
    3643            8 :                     }
    3644            8 :                     else {
    3645            8 :                         fail(Diagnostics.File_0_not_found, fileName);
    3646            8 :                     }
    3647            8 :                 }
    3648            8 :                 else if (isReferencedFile(reason) && canonicalFileName === host.getCanonicalFileName(getSourceFileByPath(reason.file)!.fileName)) {
    3649            8 :                     fail(Diagnostics.A_file_cannot_have_a_reference_to_itself);
    3650            8 :                 }
    3651            8 :             }
    3652            8 :             return sourceFile;
    3653            8 :         }
    3654            8 :         else {
    3655            8 :             const sourceFileNoExtension = options.allowNonTsExtensions && getSourceFile(fileName);
    3656            8 :             if (sourceFileNoExtension) return sourceFileNoExtension;
    3657            8 : 
    3658            8 :             if (fail && options.allowNonTsExtensions) {
    3659            8 :                 fail(Diagnostics.File_0_not_found, fileName);
    3660            8 :                 return undefined;
    3661            8 :             }
    3662            8 : 
    3663            8 :             // Only try adding extensions from the first supported group (which should be .ts/.tsx/.d.ts)
    3664            8 :             const sourceFileWithAddedExtension = forEach(supportedExtensions[0], extension => getSourceFile(fileName + extension));
    3665            8 :             if (fail && !sourceFileWithAddedExtension) fail(Diagnostics.Could_not_resolve_the_path_0_with_the_extensions_Colon_1, fileName, "'" + flatten(supportedExtensions).join("', '") + "'");
    3666            8 :             return sourceFileWithAddedExtension;
    3667            8 :         }
    3668            8 :     }
    3669            8 : 
    3670            8 :     /** This has side effects through `findSourceFile`. */

    3672            8 :         getSourceFileFromReferenceWorker(

    3675            8 :             (diagnostic, ...args) => addFilePreprocessingFileExplainingDiagnostic(/*file*/ undefined, reason, diagnostic, args),
    3676            8 :             reason,
    3677            8 :         );
    3678            8 :     }
    3679            8 :

    3681            8 :         return processSourceFile(fileName, /*isDefaultLib*/ false, /*ignoreNoDefaultLib*/ false, /*packageId*/ undefined, reason);
    3682            8 :     }

    3684            8 :     function reportFileNamesDifferOnlyInCasingError(fileName: string, existingFile: SourceFile, reason: FileIncludeReason): void {
    3685            8 :         const hasExistingReasonToReportErrorOn = !isReferencedFile(reason) && some(fileReasons.get(existingFile.path), isReferencedFile);

    3687            8 :             addFilePreprocessingFileExplainingDiagnostic(existingFile, reason, Diagnostics.Already_included_file_name_0_differs_from_file_name_1_only_in_casing, [existingFile.fileName, fileName]);

    3690            8 :             addFilePreprocessingFileExplainingDiagnostic(existingFile, reason, Diagnostics.File_name_0_differs_from_already_included_file_name_1_only_in_casing, [fileName, existingFile.fileName]);
    3691            8 :         }

    3694            8 :     function createRedirectedSourceFile(redirectTarget: SourceFile, unredirected: SourceFile, fileName: string, path: Path, resolvedPath: Path, originalFileName: string, sourceFileOptions: CreateSourceFileOptions): SourceFile {

    3706            8 :     // Get source file from normalized fileName
    3707            8 :     function findSourceFile(fileName: string, isDefaultLib: boolean, ignoreNoDefaultLib: boolean, reason: FileIncludeReason, packageId: PackageId | undefined): SourceFile | undefined {
    3708            8 :         tracing?.push(tracing.Phase.Program, "findSourceFile", {
    3709            8 :             fileName,
    3710            8 :             isDefaultLib: isDefaultLib || undefined,
    3711            8 :             fileIncludeKind: (FileIncludeKind as any)[reason.kind],
    3712            8 :         });
    3713            8 :         const result = findSourceFileWorker(fileName, isDefaultLib, ignoreNoDefaultLib, reason, packageId);
    3714            8 :         tracing?.pop();
    3715            8 :         return result;
    3716            8 :     }
    3717            8 : 
    3718            8 :     function getCreateSourceFileOptions(fileName: string, moduleResolutionCache: ModuleResolutionCache | undefined, host: CompilerHost, options: CompilerOptions): CreateSourceFileOptions {
    3719            8 :         // It's a _little odd_ that we can't set `impliedNodeFormat` until the program step - but it's the first and only time we have a resolution cache
    3720            8 :         // and a freshly made source file node on hand at the same time, and we need both to set the field. Persisting the resolution cache all the way
    3721            8 :         // to the check and emit steps would be bad - so we much prefer detecting and storing the format information on the source file node upfront.
    3722            8 :         const result = getImpliedNodeFormatForFileWorker(getNormalizedAbsolutePath(fileName, currentDirectory), moduleResolutionCache?.getPackageJsonInfoCache(), host, options);
    3723            8 :         const languageVersion = getEmitScriptTarget(options);
    3724            8 :         const setExternalModuleIndicator = getSetExternalModuleIndicator(options);
    3725            8 :         return typeof result === "object" ?
    3726            8 :             { ...result, languageVersion, setExternalModuleIndicator, jsDocParsingMode: host.jsDocParsingMode } :
    3727            8 :             { languageVersion, impliedNodeFormat: result, setExternalModuleIndicator, jsDocParsingMode: host.jsDocParsingMode };
    3728            8 :     }
    3729            8 : 
    3730            8 :     function findSourceFileWorker(fileName: string, isDefaultLib: boolean, ignoreNoDefaultLib: boolean, reason: FileIncludeReason, packageId: PackageId | undefined): SourceFile | undefined {
    3731            8 :         const path = toPath(fileName);
    3732            8 :         if (useSourceOfProjectReferenceRedirect) {
    3733            8 :             let source = getSourceOfProjectReferenceRedirect(path);
    3734            8 :             // If preserveSymlinks is true, module resolution wont jump the symlink
    3735            8 :             // but the resolved real path may be the .d.ts from project reference
    3736            8 :             // Note:: Currently we try the real path only if the
    3737            8 :             // file is from node_modules to avoid having to run real path on all file paths
    3738            8 :             if (
    3739            8 :                 !source &&
    3740            8 :                 host.realpath &&
    3741            8 :                 options.preserveSymlinks &&
    3742            8 :                 isDeclarationFileName(fileName) &&
    3743            8 :                 fileName.includes(nodeModulesPathPart)
    3744            8 :             ) {
    3745            8 :                 const realPath = toPath(host.realpath(fileName));
    3746            8 :                 if (realPath !== path) source = getSourceOfProjectReferenceRedirect(realPath);
    3747            8 :             }
    3748            8 :             if (source) {
    3749            8 :                 const file = isString(source) ?
    3750            8 :                     findSourceFile(source, isDefaultLib, ignoreNoDefaultLib, reason, packageId) :
    3751            8 :                     undefined;
    3752            8 :                 if (file) addFileToFilesByName(file, path, fileName, /*redirectedPath*/ undefined);
    3753            8 :                 return file;
    3754            8 :             }
    3755            8 :         }
    3756            8 :         const originalFileName = fileName;
    3757            8 :         if (filesByName.has(path)) {
    3758            8 :             const file = filesByName.get(path);
    3759            8 :             const addedReason = addFileIncludeReason(file || undefined, reason, /*checkExisting*/ true);
    3760            8 :             // try to check if we've already seen this file but with a different casing in path
    3761            8 :             // NOTE: this only makes sense for case-insensitive file systems, and only on files which are not redirected
    3762            8 :             if (file && addedReason && !(options.forceConsistentCasingInFileNames === false)) {
    3763            8 :                 const checkedName = file.fileName;
    3764            8 :                 const isRedirect = toPath(checkedName) !== toPath(fileName);
    3765            8 :                 if (isRedirect) {
    3766            8 :                     fileName = getProjectReferenceRedirect(fileName) || fileName;
    3767            8 :                 }
    3768            8 :                 // Check if it differs only in drive letters its ok to ignore that error:
    3769            8 :                 const checkedAbsolutePath = getNormalizedAbsolutePathWithoutRoot(checkedName, currentDirectory);
    3770            8 :                 const inputAbsolutePath = getNormalizedAbsolutePathWithoutRoot(fileName, currentDirectory);
    3771            8 :                 if (checkedAbsolutePath !== inputAbsolutePath) {
    3772            8 :                     reportFileNamesDifferOnlyInCasingError(fileName, file, reason);
    3773            8 :                 }
    3774            8 :             }
    3775            8 : 
    3776            8 :             // If the file was previously found via a node_modules search, but is now being processed as a root file,
    3777            8 :             // then everything it sucks in may also be marked incorrectly, and needs to be checked again.
    3778            8 :             if (file && sourceFilesFoundSearchingNodeModules.get(file.path) && currentNodeModulesDepth === 0) {
    3779            8 :                 sourceFilesFoundSearchingNodeModules.set(file.path, false);
    3780            8 :                 if (!options.noResolve) {
    3781            8 :                     processReferencedFiles(file, isDefaultLib);
    3782            8 :                     processTypeReferenceDirectives(file);
    3783            8 :                 }
    3784            8 :                 if (!options.noLib) {
    3785            8 :                     processLibReferenceDirectives(file);
    3786            8 :                 }
    3787            8 : 
    3788            8 :                 modulesWithElidedImports.set(file.path, false);
    3789            8 :                 processImportedModules(file);
    3790            8 :             }
    3791            8 :             // See if we need to reprocess the imports due to prior skipped imports
    3792            8 :             else if (file && modulesWithElidedImports.get(file.path)) {
    3793            8 :                 if (currentNodeModulesDepth < maxNodeModuleJsDepth) {
    3794            8 :                     modulesWithElidedImports.set(file.path, false);
    3795            8 :                     processImportedModules(file);
    3796            8 :                 }
    3797            8 :             }
    3798            8 : 
    3799            8 :             return file || undefined;
    3800            8 :         }
    3801            8 : 
    3802            8 :         let redirectedPath: Path | undefined;
    3803            8 :         if (!useSourceOfProjectReferenceRedirect) {
    3804            8 :             const redirectProject = getProjectReferenceRedirectProject(fileName);
    3805            8 :             if (redirectProject) {
    3806            8 :                 if (redirectProject.commandLine.options.outFile) {
    3807            8 :                     // Shouldnt create many to 1 mapping file in --out scenario
    3808            8 :                     return undefined;
    3809            8 :                 }
    3810            8 :                 const redirect = getProjectReferenceOutputName(redirectProject, fileName);
    3811            8 :                 fileName = redirect;
    3812            8 :                 // Once we start redirecting to a file, we can potentially come back to it
    3813            8 :                 // via a back-reference from another file in the .d.ts folder. If that happens we'll
    3814            8 :                 // end up trying to add it to the program *again* because we were tracking it via its
    3815            8 :                 // original (un-redirected) name. So we have to map both the original path and the redirected path
    3816            8 :                 // to the source file we're about to find/create
    3817            8 :                 redirectedPath = toPath(redirect);
    3818            8 :             }
    3819            8 :         }
    3820            8 : 
    3821            8 :         // We haven't looked for this file, do so now and cache result
    3822            8 :         const sourceFileOptions = getCreateSourceFileOptions(fileName, moduleResolutionCache, host, options);
    3823            8 :         const file = host.getSourceFile(
    3824            8 :             fileName,
    3825            8 :             sourceFileOptions,
    3826            8 :             hostErrorMessage => addFilePreprocessingFileExplainingDiagnostic(/*file*/ undefined, reason, Diagnostics.Cannot_read_file_0_Colon_1, [fileName, hostErrorMessage]),
    3827            8 :             shouldCreateNewSourceFile,
    3828            8 :         );
    3829            8 : 
    3830            8 :         if (packageId) {
    3831            8 :             const packageIdKey = packageIdToString(packageId);
    3832            8 :             const fileFromPackageId = packageIdToSourceFile.get(packageIdKey);
    3833            8 :             if (fileFromPackageId) {
    3834            8 :                 // Some other SourceFile already exists with this package name and version.
    3835            8 :                 // Instead of creating a duplicate, just redirect to the existing one.
    3836            8 :                 const dupFile = createRedirectedSourceFile(fileFromPackageId, file!, fileName, path, toPath(fileName), originalFileName, sourceFileOptions);
    3837            8 :                 redirectTargetsMap.add(fileFromPackageId.path, fileName);
    3838            8 :                 addFileToFilesByName(dupFile, path, fileName, redirectedPath);
    3839            8 :                 addFileIncludeReason(dupFile, reason, /*checkExisting*/ false);
    3840            8 :                 sourceFileToPackageName.set(path, packageIdToPackageName(packageId));
    3841            8 :                 processingOtherFiles!.push(dupFile);
    3842            8 :                 return dupFile;
    3843            8 :             }
    3844            8 :             else if (file) {
    3845            8 :                 // This is the first source file to have this packageId.
    3846            8 :                 packageIdToSourceFile.set(packageIdKey, file);
    3847            8 :                 sourceFileToPackageName.set(path, packageIdToPackageName(packageId));
    3848            8 :             }
    3849            8 :         }
    3850            8 :         addFileToFilesByName(file, path, fileName, redirectedPath);
    3851            8 : 
    3852            8 :         if (file) {
    3853            8 :             sourceFilesFoundSearchingNodeModules.set(path, currentNodeModulesDepth > 0);

    4146            8 :     function processImportedModules(file: SourceFile) {
    4147            8 :         collectExternalModuleReferences(file);

    4156            8 :             (resolvedModules ??= new Map()).set(file.path, resolutionsInFile);
    4157            8 :             for (let index = 0; index < moduleNames.length; index++) {

    4163            8 : 
    4164            8 :                 if (!resolution) {
    4165            8 :                     continue;
