    4167            8 : 
    4168            8 :                 const isFromNodeModulesSearch = resolution.isExternalLibraryImport;

    4181            8 :                 // - module name comes from the list of imports
    4182            8 :                 // - it's not a top level JavaScript module that exceeded the search max
    4183            8 :                 const elideImport = isJsFileFromNodeModules && currentNodeModulesDepth > maxNodeModuleJsDepth;

    4187            8 :                     && !getResolutionDiagnostic(optionsForFile, resolution, file)

    4234            8 :     function parseProjectReferenceConfigFile(ref: ProjectReference): ResolvedProjectReference | undefined {
    4235            8 :         if (!projectReferenceRedirects) {
    4236            8 :             projectReferenceRedirects = new Map();
    4237            8 :         }
    4238            8 : 
    4239            8 :         // The actual filename (i.e. add "/tsconfig.json" if necessary)
    4240            8 :         const refPath = resolveProjectReferencePath(ref);
    4241            8 :         const sourceFilePath = toPath(refPath);
    4242            8 :         const fromCache = projectReferenceRedirects.get(sourceFilePath);
    4243            8 :         if (fromCache !== undefined) {
    4244            8 :             return fromCache || undefined;
    4245            8 :         }
    4246            8 : 
    4247            8 :         let commandLine: ParsedCommandLine | undefined;
    4248            8 :         let sourceFile: JsonSourceFile | undefined;
    4249            8 :         if (host.getParsedCommandLine) {
    4250            8 :             commandLine = host.getParsedCommandLine(refPath);
    4251            8 :             if (!commandLine) {
    4252            8 :                 addFileToFilesByName(/*file*/ undefined, sourceFilePath, refPath, /*redirectedPath*/ undefined);
    4253            8 :                 projectReferenceRedirects.set(sourceFilePath, false);
    4254            8 :                 return undefined;
    4255            8 :             }
    4256            8 :             sourceFile = Debug.checkDefined(commandLine.options.configFile);
    4257            8 :             Debug.assert(!sourceFile.path || sourceFile.path === sourceFilePath);
    4258            8 :             addFileToFilesByName(sourceFile, sourceFilePath, refPath, /*redirectedPath*/ undefined);
    4259            8 :         }
    4260            8 :         else {
    4261            8 :             // An absolute path pointing to the containing directory of the config file
    4262            8 :             const basePath = getNormalizedAbsolutePath(getDirectoryPath(refPath), currentDirectory);
    4263            8 :             sourceFile = host.getSourceFile(refPath, ScriptTarget.JSON) as JsonSourceFile | undefined;
    4264            8 :             addFileToFilesByName(sourceFile, sourceFilePath, refPath, /*redirectedPath*/ undefined);
    4265            8 :             if (sourceFile === undefined) {
    4266            8 :                 projectReferenceRedirects.set(sourceFilePath, false);
    4267            8 :                 return undefined;
    4268            8 :             }
    4269            8 :             commandLine = parseJsonSourceFileConfigFileContent(sourceFile, configParsingHost, basePath, /*existingOptions*/ undefined, refPath);
    4270            8 :         }
    4271            8 :         sourceFile.fileName = refPath;
    4272            8 :         sourceFile.path = sourceFilePath;
    4273            8 :         sourceFile.resolvedPath = sourceFilePath;
    4274            8 :         sourceFile.originalFileName = refPath;
    4275            8 : 
    4276            8 :         const resolvedRef: ResolvedProjectReference = { commandLine, sourceFile };
    4277            8 :         projectReferenceRedirects.set(sourceFilePath, resolvedRef);

    4279            8 :             resolvedRef.references = commandLine.projectReferences.map(parseProjectReferenceConfigFile);
    4280            8 :         }

    4623            8 :     function getIgnoreDeprecationsVersion(): Version {
    4624            8 :         const ignoreDeprecations = options.ignoreDeprecations;
    4625            8 :         if (ignoreDeprecations) {
    4626            8 :             // While we could do Version.tryParse here to support any version,
    4627            8 :             // for now, only allow "5.0". We aren't planning on deprecating anything
    4628            8 :             // until 6.0.
    4629            8 :             if (ignoreDeprecations === "5.0") {
    4630            8 :                 return new Version(ignoreDeprecations);
    4631            8 :             }
    4632            8 :             reportInvalidIgnoreDeprecations();
    4633            8 :         }
    4634            8 :         return Version.zero;
    4635            8 :     }
    4636            8 : 
    4637            8 :     function checkDeprecations(
    4638            8 :         deprecatedIn: string,
    4639            8 :         removedIn: string,
    4640            8 :         createDiagnostic: (name: string, value: string | undefined, useInstead: string | undefined, message: DiagnosticMessage, ...args: DiagnosticArguments) => void,
    4641            8 :         fn: (createDeprecatedDiagnostic: (name: string, value?: string, useInstead?: string) => void) => void,
    4642            8 :     ) {
    4643            8 :         const deprecatedInVersion = new Version(deprecatedIn);
    4644            8 :         const removedInVersion = new Version(removedIn);
    4645            8 :         const typescriptVersion = new Version(typeScriptVersion || versionMajorMinor);
    4646            8 :         const ignoreDeprecationsVersion = getIgnoreDeprecationsVersion();
    4647            8 : 
    4648            8 :         const mustBeRemoved = !(removedInVersion.compareTo(typescriptVersion) === Comparison.GreaterThan);
    4649            8 :         const canBeSilenced = !mustBeRemoved && ignoreDeprecationsVersion.compareTo(deprecatedInVersion) === Comparison.LessThan;
    4650            8 : 
    4651            8 :         if (mustBeRemoved || canBeSilenced) {
    4652            8 :             fn((name, value, useInstead) => {
    4653            8 :                 if (mustBeRemoved) {
    4654            8 :                     if (value === undefined) {
    4655            8 :                         createDiagnostic(name, value, useInstead, Diagnostics.Option_0_has_been_removed_Please_remove_it_from_your_configuration, name);
    4656            8 :                     }
    4657            8 :                     else {
    4658            8 :                         createDiagnostic(name, value, useInstead, Diagnostics.Option_0_1_has_been_removed_Please_remove_it_from_your_configuration, name, value);
    4659            8 :                     }
    4660            8 :                 }
    4661            8 :                 else {
    4662            8 :                     if (value === undefined) {
    4663            8 :                         createDiagnostic(name, value, useInstead, Diagnostics.Option_0_is_deprecated_and_will_stop_functioning_in_TypeScript_1_Specify_compilerOption_ignoreDeprecations_Colon_2_to_silence_this_error, name, removedIn, deprecatedIn);
    4664            8 :                     }
    4665            8 :                     else {
    4666            8 :                         createDiagnostic(name, value, useInstead, Diagnostics.Option_0_1_is_deprecated_and_will_stop_functioning_in_TypeScript_2_Specify_compilerOption_ignoreDeprecations_Colon_3_to_silence_this_error, name, value, removedIn, deprecatedIn);
    4667            8 :                     }
    4668            8 :                 }
    4669            8 :             });
    4670            8 :         }
    4671            8 :     }
    4672            8 :

    4731            8 :     function createDiagnosticExplainingFile(file: SourceFile | undefined, fileProcessingReason: FileIncludeReason | undefined, diagnostic: DiagnosticMessage, args: DiagnosticArguments): Diagnostic {
    4732            8 :         let seenReasons: Set<FileIncludeReason> | undefined;
    4733            8 :         const reasons = file && fileReasons.get(file.path);
    4734            8 :         let fileIncludeReasons: DiagnosticMessageChain[] | undefined;
    4735            8 :         let relatedInfo: DiagnosticWithLocation[] | undefined;
    4736            8 :         let locationReason = isReferencedFile(fileProcessingReason) ? fileProcessingReason : undefined;
    4737            8 :         let fileIncludeReasonDetails: DiagnosticMessageChain | undefined;
    4738            8 :         let redirectInfo: DiagnosticMessageChain[] | undefined;
    4739            8 :         let cachedChain = file && fileReasonsToChain?.get(file.path);
    4740            8 :         let chain: DiagnosticMessageChain | undefined;
    4741            8 :         if (cachedChain) {
    4742            8 :             if (cachedChain.fileIncludeReasonDetails) {
    4743            8 :                 seenReasons = new Set(reasons);
    4744            8 :                 reasons?.forEach(populateRelatedInfo);
    4745            8 :             }
    4746            8 :             else {
    4747            8 :                 reasons?.forEach(processReason);
    4748            8 :             }
    4749            8 :             redirectInfo = cachedChain.redirectInfo;
    4750            8 :         }
    4751            8 :         else {
    4752            8 :             reasons?.forEach(processReason);
    4753            8 :             redirectInfo = file && explainIfFileIsRedirectAndImpliedFormat(file, getCompilerOptionsForFile(file));
    4754            8 :         }
    4755            8 : 
    4756            8 :         if (fileProcessingReason) processReason(fileProcessingReason);
    4757            8 :         const processedExtraReason = seenReasons?.size !== reasons?.length;
    4758            8 : 
    4759            8 :         // If we have location and there is only one reason file is in which is the location, dont add details for file include
    4760            8 :         if (locationReason && seenReasons?.size === 1) seenReasons = undefined;
    4761            8 : 
    4762            8 :         if (seenReasons && cachedChain) {
    4763            8 :             if (cachedChain.details && !processedExtraReason) {
    4764            8 :                 chain = chainDiagnosticMessages(cachedChain.details, diagnostic, ...args || emptyArray);
    4765            8 :             }
    4766            8 :             else if (cachedChain.fileIncludeReasonDetails) {
    4767            8 :                 if (!processedExtraReason) {
    4768            8 :                     if (!cachedFileIncludeDetailsHasProcessedExtraReason()) {
    4769            8 :                         fileIncludeReasonDetails = cachedChain.fileIncludeReasonDetails;
    4770            8 :                     }
    4771            8 :                     else {
    4772            8 :                         fileIncludeReasons = cachedChain.fileIncludeReasonDetails.next!.slice(0, reasons!.length);
    4773            8 :                     }
    4774            8 :                 }
    4775            8 :                 else {
    4776            8 :                     if (!cachedFileIncludeDetailsHasProcessedExtraReason()) {
    4777            8 :                         fileIncludeReasons = [...cachedChain.fileIncludeReasonDetails.next!, fileIncludeReasons![0]];
    4778            8 :                     }
    4779            8 :                     else {
    4780            8 :                         fileIncludeReasons = append(cachedChain.fileIncludeReasonDetails.next!.slice(0, reasons!.length), fileIncludeReasons![0]);
    4781            8 :                     }
    4782            8 :                 }
    4783            8 :             }
    4784            8 :         }
    4785            8 : 
    4786            8 :         if (!chain) {
    4787            8 :             if (!fileIncludeReasonDetails) fileIncludeReasonDetails = seenReasons && chainDiagnosticMessages(fileIncludeReasons, Diagnostics.The_file_is_in_the_program_because_Colon);
    4788            8 :             chain = chainDiagnosticMessages(
    4789            8 :                 redirectInfo ?
    4790            8 :                     fileIncludeReasonDetails ? [fileIncludeReasonDetails, ...redirectInfo] : redirectInfo :
    4791            8 :                     fileIncludeReasonDetails,
    4792            8 :                 diagnostic,
    4793            8 :                 ...args || emptyArray,
    4794            8 :             );
    4795            8 :         }
    4796            8 : 
    4797            8 :         // This is chain's next contains:
    4798            8 :         //   - File is in program because:
    4799            8 :         //      - Files reasons listed
    4800            8 :         //      - extra reason if its not already processed - this happens in case sensitive file system where files differ in casing and we are giving reasons for two files so reason is not in file's reason
    4801            8 :         //     fyi above whole secton is ommited if we have single reason and we are reporting at that reason's location
    4802            8 :         //   - redirect and additional information about file
    4803            8 :         // So cache result if we havent ommited file include reasons
    4804            8 :         if (file) {
    4805            8 :             if (cachedChain) {
    4806            8 :                 // Cache new fileIncludeDetails if we have update
    4807            8 :                 // Or if we had cached with more details than the reasons
    4808            8 :                 if (!cachedChain.fileIncludeReasonDetails || (!processedExtraReason && fileIncludeReasonDetails)) {
    4809            8 :                     cachedChain.fileIncludeReasonDetails = fileIncludeReasonDetails;
    4810            8 :                 }
    4811            8 :             }
    4812            8 :             else {
    4813            8 :                 (fileReasonsToChain ??= new Map()).set(file.path, cachedChain = { fileIncludeReasonDetails, redirectInfo });
    4814            8 :             }
    4815            8 :             // If we didnt compute extra file include reason , cache the details to use directly
    4816            8 :             if (!cachedChain.details && !processedExtraReason) cachedChain.details = chain.next;
    4817            8 :         }
    4818            8 : 
    4819            8 :         const location = locationReason && getReferencedFileLocation(program, locationReason);
    4820            8 :         return location && isReferenceFileLocation(location) ?
    4821            8 :             createFileDiagnosticFromMessageChain(location.file, location.pos, location.end - location.pos, chain, relatedInfo) :
    4822            8 :             createCompilerDiagnosticFromMessageChain(chain, relatedInfo);
    4823            8 : 
    4824            8 :         function processReason(reason: FileIncludeReason) {
    4825            8 :             if (seenReasons?.has(reason)) return;
    4826            8 :             (seenReasons ??= new Set()).add(reason);
    4827            8 :             (fileIncludeReasons ??= []).push(fileIncludeReasonToDiagnostics(program, reason));
    4828            8 :             populateRelatedInfo(reason);
    4829            8 :         }
    4830            8 : 
    4831            8 :         function populateRelatedInfo(reason: FileIncludeReason) {
    4832            8 :             if (!locationReason && isReferencedFile(reason)) {
    4833            8 :                 // Report error at first reference file or file currently in processing and dont report in related information
    4834            8 :                 locationReason = reason;
    4835            8 :             }
    4836            8 :             else if (locationReason !== reason) {
    4837            8 :                 relatedInfo = append(relatedInfo, getFileIncludeReasonToRelatedInformation(reason));
    4838            8 :             }
    4839            8 :         }
    4840            8 : 
    4841            8 :         function cachedFileIncludeDetailsHasProcessedExtraReason() {
    4842            8 :             return cachedChain!.fileIncludeReasonDetails!.next?.length !== reasons?.length;
    4843            8 :         }
    4844            8 :     }
    4845            8 :

    4860            8 :     function getFileIncludeReasonToRelatedInformation(reason: FileIncludeReason) {

    4866            8 :     function fileIncludeReasonToRelatedInformation(reason: FileIncludeReason): DiagnosticWithLocation | undefined {
    4867            8 :         if (isReferencedFile(reason)) {
    4868            8 :             const referenceLocation = getReferencedFileLocation(program, reason);
    4869            8 :             let message: DiagnosticMessage;
    4870            8 :             switch (reason.kind) {
    4871            8 :                 case FileIncludeKind.Import:
    4872            8 :                     message = Diagnostics.File_is_included_via_import_here;
    4873            8 :                     break;
    4874            8 :                 case FileIncludeKind.ReferenceFile:
    4875            8 :                     message = Diagnostics.File_is_included_via_reference_here;
    4876            8 :                     break;
    4877            8 :                 case FileIncludeKind.TypeReferenceDirective:
    4878            8 :                     message = Diagnostics.File_is_included_via_type_library_reference_here;
    4879            8 :                     break;
    4880            8 :                 case FileIncludeKind.LibReferenceDirective:
    4881            8 :                     message = Diagnostics.File_is_included_via_library_reference_here;
    4882            8 :                     break;
    4883            8 :                 default:
    4884            8 :                     Debug.assertNever(reason);
    4885            8 :             }
    4886            8 :             return isReferenceFileLocation(referenceLocation) ? createFileDiagnostic(
    4887            8 :                 referenceLocation.file,
    4888            8 :                 referenceLocation.pos,
    4889            8 :                 referenceLocation.end - referenceLocation.pos,
    4890            8 :                 message,
    4891            8 :             ) : undefined;
    4892            8 :         }
    4893            8 : 
    4894            8 :         if (!options.configFile) return undefined;
    4895            8 :         let configFileNode: Node | undefined;
    4896            8 :         let message: DiagnosticMessage;
    4897            8 :         switch (reason.kind) {
    4898            8 :             case FileIncludeKind.RootFile:
    4899            8 :                 if (!options.configFile.configFileSpecs) return undefined;
    4900            8 :                 const fileName = getNormalizedAbsolutePath(rootNames[reason.index], currentDirectory);
    4901            8 :                 const matchedByFiles = getMatchedFileSpec(program, fileName);
    4902            8 :                 if (matchedByFiles) {
    4903            8 :                     configFileNode = getTsConfigPropArrayElementValue(options.configFile, "files", matchedByFiles);
    4904            8 :                     message = Diagnostics.File_is_matched_by_files_list_specified_here;
    4905            8 :                     break;
    4906            8 :                 }
    4907            8 :                 const matchedByInclude = getMatchedIncludeSpec(program, fileName);
    4908            8 :                 // Could be additional files specified as roots
    4909            8 :                 if (!matchedByInclude || !isString(matchedByInclude)) return undefined;
    4910            8 :                 configFileNode = getTsConfigPropArrayElementValue(options.configFile, "include", matchedByInclude);
    4911            8 :                 message = Diagnostics.File_is_matched_by_include_pattern_specified_here;
    4912            8 :                 break;
    4913            8 :             case FileIncludeKind.SourceFromProjectReference:
    4914            8 :             case FileIncludeKind.OutputFromProjectReference:
    4915            8 :                 const referencedResolvedRef = Debug.checkDefined(resolvedProjectReferences?.[reason.index]);
    4916            8 :                 const referenceInfo = forEachProjectReference(projectReferences, resolvedProjectReferences, (resolvedRef, parent, index) => resolvedRef === referencedResolvedRef ? { sourceFile: parent?.sourceFile || options.configFile!, index } : undefined);
    4917            8 :                 if (!referenceInfo) return undefined;
    4918            8 :                 const { sourceFile, index } = referenceInfo;
    4919            8 :                 const referencesSyntax = forEachTsConfigPropArray(sourceFile as TsConfigSourceFile, "references", property => isArrayLiteralExpression(property.initializer) ? property.initializer : undefined);
    4920            8 :                 return referencesSyntax && referencesSyntax.elements.length > index ?
    4921            8 :                     createDiagnosticForNodeInSourceFile(
    4922            8 :                         sourceFile,
    4923            8 :                         referencesSyntax.elements[index],
    4924            8 :                         reason.kind === FileIncludeKind.OutputFromProjectReference ?
    4925            8 :                             Diagnostics.File_is_output_from_referenced_project_specified_here :
    4926            8 :                             Diagnostics.File_is_source_from_referenced_project_specified_here,
    4927            8 :                     ) :
    4928            8 :                     undefined;
    4929            8 :             case FileIncludeKind.AutomaticTypeDirectiveFile:
    4930            8 :                 if (!options.types) return undefined;
    4931            8 :                 configFileNode = getOptionsSyntaxByArrayElementValue("types", reason.typeReference);
    4932            8 :                 message = Diagnostics.File_is_entry_point_of_type_library_specified_here;
    4933            8 :                 break;
    4934            8 :             case FileIncludeKind.LibFile:
    4935            8 :                 if (reason.index !== undefined) {
    4936            8 :                     configFileNode = getOptionsSyntaxByArrayElementValue("lib", options.lib![reason.index]);
    4937            8 :                     message = Diagnostics.File_is_library_specified_here;
    4938            8 :                     break;
    4939            8 :                 }
    4940            8 :                 const target = getNameOfScriptTarget(getEmitScriptTarget(options));
    4941            8 :                 configFileNode = target ? getOptionsSyntaxByValue("target", target) : undefined;
    4942            8 :                 message = Diagnostics.File_is_default_library_for_target_specified_here;
    4943            8 :                 break;
    4944            8 :             default:
    4945            8 :                 Debug.assertNever(reason);
    4946            8 :         }
    4947            8 :         return configFileNode && createDiagnosticForNodeInSourceFile(
    4948            8 :             options.configFile,
    4949            8 :             configFileNode,
    4950            8 :             message,
    4951            8 :         );
    4952            8 :     }
